#### Release Body

# v0.28.0 — core Blueprint authoring + playable-character closure + runtime verification

## English

v0.28.0 fills the core Blueprint authoring layer and adds runtime verification, so AI can build a genuinely playable third-person character end-to-end using visible core `unreal.*` tools only, with no `execute_python` fallback. In dogfood testing, `pie_input_probe` measured about **126 cm** of forward movement through input-layer injection driving the bound Blueprint graph.

Ten new core tools bring the registry from **164 to 174**:

- **Input events**: `unreal.bp_add_input_axis_event_node` and `unreal.bp_add_input_action_event_node` create legacy K2 input-event nodes.
- **Blueprint SCS components**: `unreal.bp_add_component` and `unreal.bp_set_component_property` add Blueprint Simple Construction Script components such as SpringArm, Camera, or any SceneComponent, with allowlisted property writes.
- **Class defaults / level / possession**: `unreal.bp_set_class_default`, `unreal.editor_set_map_game_mode`, and `unreal.actor_set_auto_possess` wire class defaults such as `GameMode.DefaultPawnClass`, current-map GameMode override, and Player0 possession.
- **Gameplay graph nodes**: `unreal.bp_add_gameplay_node` exposes a curated enum for AddMovementInput, AddControllerYawInput, AddControllerPitchInput, GetActorForwardVector, GetActorRightVector, GetControlRotation, Jump, and FloatGreaterThan.
- **Runtime verification**: `unreal.pie_input_probe` asynchronously injects input in PIE and measures pawn displacement using FTSTicker without pumping the editor tick from a handler; `unreal.verify_viewport_widgets` read-only checks UMG widgets on the viewport.

Additional fixes and architecture notes: `unreal.configure_player_input` now accepts arbitrary legacy axis/action mapping names; `unreal.bp_set_pin_default` no longer false-fails its postcheck for object/class default pins; the implementation heavily reuses the existing `UnrealMcpBlueprintGraphLibrary` and adds `UnrealMcpBlueprintComponentLibrary`; and the v0.27.1 `unreal.verify_player_controls` crash fix is included, avoiding re-entrant editor ticks from the handler. The same source tree is validated for Unreal Engine **5.6 and 5.7**.

## 中文

v0.28.0 补齐核心蓝图创作层并新增运行时验证，让 AI 现在可以只用可见核心 `unreal.*` 工具端到端造出真正可玩的第三人称角色，且不再需要退回 `execute_python`。在 dogfood 验证中，`pie_input_probe` 通过输入层注入触发绑定的蓝图图表，量得前进约 **126 cm**。

本版新增 10 个核心工具，注册表总数从 **164 增至 174**：

- **输入事件**：`unreal.bp_add_input_axis_event_node` 与 `unreal.bp_add_input_action_event_node` 创建 legacy K2 输入事件节点。
- **蓝图 SCS 组件**：`unreal.bp_add_component` 与 `unreal.bp_set_component_property` 添加 Blueprint Simple Construction Script 组件，例如 SpringArm、Camera 或任意 SceneComponent，并通过 allowlist 限定属性写入。
- **类默认 / 关卡 / possess**：`unreal.bp_set_class_default`、`unreal.editor_set_map_game_mode` 与 `unreal.actor_set_auto_possess` 负责 `GameMode.DefaultPawnClass` 等类默认值、当前地图 GameMode override，以及 Player0 possess。
- **gameplay 图节点**：`unreal.bp_add_gameplay_node` 提供经过收敛的枚举：AddMovementInput、AddControllerYawInput、AddControllerPitchInput、GetActorForwardVector、GetActorRightVector、GetControlRotation、Jump、FloatGreaterThan。
- **运行时验证**：`unreal.pie_input_probe` 在 PIE 中异步注入输入并量测 pawn 位移，使用 FTSTicker 驱动，不从 handler 泵编辑器 tick；`unreal.verify_viewport_widgets` 只读检查 viewport 上的 UMG widget。

其他修复与架构说明：`unreal.configure_player_input` 现在接受任意 legacy 轴/动作映射名；`unreal.bp_set_pin_default` 修复了 object/class 默认引脚 postcheck 的误报；实现大量复用既有 `UnrealMcpBlueprintGraphLibrary`，并新增 `UnrealMcpBlueprintComponentLibrary`；同时并入 v0.27.1 的 `unreal.verify_player_controls` 崩溃修复，避免 handler 重入编辑器 tick。同一份 source 已在 Unreal Engine **5.6 与 5.7** 上验证。

## 日本語

v0.28.0 は core Blueprint authoring layer を補完し、runtime verification を追加します。AI は visible core `unreal.*` tool だけで、`execute_python` に頼らず、真に playable な third-person character を end-to-end で構築できるようになりました。dogfood 検証では、`pie_input_probe` が input layer 注入で bound Blueprint graph を駆動し、約 **126 cm** の前進を計測しました。

このリリースでは core tool を 10 個追加し、registry 総数は **164 から 174** になりました：

- **Input events**：`unreal.bp_add_input_axis_event_node` と `unreal.bp_add_input_action_event_node` が legacy K2 input-event node を作成します。
- **Blueprint SCS components**：`unreal.bp_add_component` と `unreal.bp_set_component_property` が SpringArm、Camera、任意の SceneComponent などの Blueprint Simple Construction Script component を追加し、allowlist 付きで property を書き込みます。
- **Class defaults / level / possession**：`unreal.bp_set_class_default`、`unreal.editor_set_map_game_mode`、`unreal.actor_set_auto_possess` が `GameMode.DefaultPawnClass` などの class default、現在マップの GameMode override、Player0 possession を設定します。
- **Gameplay graph nodes**：`unreal.bp_add_gameplay_node` は AddMovementInput、AddControllerYawInput、AddControllerPitchInput、GetActorForwardVector、GetActorRightVector、GetControlRotation、Jump、FloatGreaterThan の curated enum を提供します。
- **Runtime verification**：`unreal.pie_input_probe` は PIE 内で input を非同期注入し、FTSTicker 駆動で pawn の変位を計測します（handler から editor tick を pump しません）；`unreal.verify_viewport_widgets` は viewport 上の UMG widget を read-only で確認します。

その他の修正と設計メモ：`unreal.configure_player_input` は任意の legacy axis/action mapping name を受け付けるようになりました；`unreal.bp_set_pin_default` は object/class default pin に対する postcheck の誤検知を修正しました；実装は既存の `UnrealMcpBlueprintGraphLibrary` を大きく再利用し、新たに `UnrealMcpBlueprintComponentLibrary` を追加しています；さらに v0.27.1 の `unreal.verify_player_controls` crash fix を取り込み、handler から editor tick に再入しないようにしました。同一ソースツリーを Unreal Engine **5.6 と 5.7** の両方で検証済みです。

## Install / 安装 / インストール

English:
Extract the source-only projectroot zip into your `<UserProject>/` root, next to the `.uproject` file — **do not** extract it under `<UserProject>/Plugins/`. The release includes both macOS and Windows source-only projectroot zips for UE 5.6 / UE 5.7; UBT compiles the plugin for your project on first editor launch or when you build the editor target.

中文：
把 source-only projectroot zip 解压到 `<UserProject>/` 根目录，也就是 `.uproject` 同级目录——**不要**解压到 `<UserProject>/Plugins/` 下面。本 release 同时提供 macOS 与 Windows 的 source-only projectroot zip，面向 UE 5.6 / UE 5.7；首次启动编辑器或构建 editor target 时，UBT 会为你的项目编译插件。

日本語：
source-only projectroot zip を `<UserProject>/` のルート、つまり `.uproject` と同じ階層に展開してください。**`<UserProject>/Plugins/` 配下には展開しないでください**。この release には UE 5.6 / UE 5.7 向けの macOS と Windows の source-only projectroot zip が含まれています。初回エディタ起動時、または editor target のビルド時に、UBT がそのプロジェクト向けに plugin をコンパイルします。

## Known limitations / 已知限制 / 既知の制限

English:
- `unreal.pie_input_probe` currently falls back to a direct call for InputAction jump verification, so jump is weaker proof than the axis-movement path; forward/backward movement is verified through input-layer injection.
- `UnrealMcp.AutomationTools.RunRecoversStale` has been a pre-existing failure since v0.20, and `UnrealMcp.PieSmoke.MapValidation` is a long-standing flaky test. Both are unrelated to v0.28.0.

中文：
- `unreal.pie_input_probe` 对 InputAction 跳跃验证目前会退回直接调用，因此 jump 的证明弱于轴向移动路径；前进/后退移动仍通过输入层注入验证。
- `UnrealMcp.AutomationTools.RunRecoversStale` 是自 v0.20 起的 pre-existing failure，`UnrealMcp.PieSmoke.MapValidation` 是长期 flaky 测试；两者都与 v0.28.0 无关。

日本語：
- `unreal.pie_input_probe` は InputAction の jump 検証では現状 direct call に fallback するため、jump は axis movement path より弱い証明です。forward/backward movement は input-layer injection で検証されています。
- `UnrealMcp.AutomationTools.RunRecoversStale` は v0.20 以降の pre-existing failure、`UnrealMcp.PieSmoke.MapValidation` は以前からある flaky test です。どちらも v0.28.0 とは無関係です。

#### Release Body

# v0.27.0 — wall off core C++ from the AI (self-extension = Python user track only)

The AI's entire self-extension surface is now the project-local **Python user-tool track** (`scaffold_mcp_tool` python → `mcp_user_registry_reload` → `mcp_user_tool_smoke` → callable). Tools the AI makes are usable in the plugin but **never reach core**. Core C++ apply/promotion is manual, developer-only, and hidden from the AI; core-promotion stays deferred.

## Changes
- **Core-merge tools hidden from the AI.** `unreal.mcp_apply_scaffold` + `unreal.mcp_extension_pipeline` flipped `visible → legacy_hidden` (both tools.json). Runtime hiding is enforced by `ShouldExposeToolToAi`.
- **`scaffold_mcp_tool` is python-only to the AI.** The advertised `implementationTrack` is now `enum ["python"]` in both schema sources (registry tools.json + the C++ runtime schema). The handler still accepts `cpp` for manual/developer calls.
- **`workflow_run` anti-relay guard.** A workflow step naming a non-visible tool is rejected, so the AI cannot relay through `workflow_run` to reach a hidden core tool. New automation test `UnrealMcp.Workflow.HiddenToolStepRejected`.
- **Central prompt rule rewritten.** AI self-extension = the Python track only; never use `execute_python` / `execute_python_file` to modify plugin source under `Plugins/UnrealMcp/Source` or the ToolRegistry JSON (prompt-rule; a hard execute_python sandbox is a deferred follow-up).
- **3 skills merged into 1.** `karpathy-guidelines` + `mcp-capability-routing` + `mcp-self-extension` → a single `mcp-self-extension` skill (MIT attribution kept).
- Docs refreshed (README ×2, SecurityModel, SelfExtensionPipeline, agents-guide, tool-docs); the incident core-C++ scaffold removed.

## Compatibility
- Tool count unchanged **162** (visible 152→150, hidden 10→12). No provider / settings / approval-gate / ChatPanel / `EAiProviderKind` change.
- Validators 162/162/0; UE 5.6 compat 0 errors / 0 warnings.
- Dual-engine: build + **50/50 curated automation** on both UE 5.6 and UE 5.7 (incl. `AllVisibleToolsSchemaCompatible` + `HiddenToolStepRejected`).

## Verify
```

shasum -a 256 -c UnrealMcp-v0.27.0-mac-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip.sha256
# expected: ea1dc3499bd02689bf7d91eb276068a80444c2e0c2544a36105a229c730fecb8

# Windows (PowerShell)

# expected: 929e73480015206d3e5c3648049d61c186688b41927efcc4013745b9c722d259
```

# v0.26.3 — ChatPanel UX (editable model field + export Save-As)

Two pre-existing (v0.24-era) chat-panel UX defects, fixed and **manually UX-verified** in-editor.

## Fixes
- **Model selector is editable again.** The model field was an `SEditableTextBox` nested inside an `SComboBox` button, so clicking opened the dropdown instead of focusing the field — you couldn't type a model (it felt "locked"). It's now a first-class editable field; the recent-models list moved to a small separate dropdown button. Codex CLI stays hard-locked to `gpt-5.5`; CodexAppServer / OpenAI / Anthropic are editable.
- **Export to a chosen folder.** `unreal.tools.export_package` still writes to the sandboxed `Saved/UnrealMcp/Packages/` (AI path unchanged), but the **Export Tool Package** button now opens a native folder picker: pick a destination → the zip is copied there and revealed; cancel → it stays in `Saved/Packages` and that folder is revealed. Remembers your last-chosen folder.

## Compatibility
- Editor-UI only. **No tool-surface change** — registry stays **162**. No provider/approval/settings/registry change.
- Dual-engine: build + **49/49 curated automation** on both UE 5.6 and UE 5.7. Runtime UX manually verified (typeable field, folder picker + copy + reveal).

#### Release Body

# v0.26.2 — reliability patch

Two real defects found through in-editor use that the test suite had missed, plus a regression test that immediately caught an incomplete fix.

## Fixes

### 1. Provider-preset tests no longer overwrite your AI config
The legacy-migration test mutated the live settings object and called the production `SaveConfig()` path, while its cleanup guard restored the *wrong* ini file — so every build-verification run silently rewrote the example project's AI providers with test values (`gpt-test` / `test.example`). If your editor settings "reset every restart," this was why. Fix: extracted a **pure** `MakeProviderFromLegacyOpenAI()` helper and rewrote the test to assert against it — no shared-object mutation, no real config writes. Production migration behavior is byte-identical. Proven on both UE 5.6 and 5.7: a ProviderPresets run now leaves your provider config untouched.

### 2. `unreal.mcp_user_tool_smoke` is now strict-schema compatible
Its `dryRunArgs` was a free-form object (`additionalProperties:true`), which OpenAI strict function-calling rejects — breaking the v0.26 user-tool verify gate on strict providers. Changed `dryRunArgs` to a JSON-string parameter in **both** the registry JSON **and** the C++ registrar that builds the runtime schema (the first pass fixed only the JSON; the runtime schema is what mattered). Added a regression test — `UnrealMcp.Audit.AllVisibleToolsSchemaCompatible` — that audits **every visible tool** for strict-schema compatibility so this class of break can't ship again. It caught the registrar miss before release.

### Also
- Resaved `Lvl_TopDown.umap` to drop a dangling external-actor reference that logged a startup error.
- Added a manual editor-smoke checklist (`Docs/Verification.md`) for the runtime UI flows automation doesn't cover (settings survive restart / user-tool reload+smoke / audit schema-compat / export zip).

## Compatibility
- **No tool-surface change** — registry stays **162**. No ChatPanel or apply-path change.
- Dual-engine: build + **49/49 curated automation PASS** on both UE 5.6 and UE 5.7.

## Verify
```
# macOS
shasum -a 256 -c UnrealMcp-v0.26.2-mac-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip.sha256
# expected: c0a83fed9d28cb776d6d0b38556e06ddd88c2b5ef3c601ec09ba84257586987a
# Windows (PowerShell)
Get-FileHash UnrealMcp-v0.26.2-win-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip -Algorithm SHA256
```
Full trilingual notes: `Docs/Release-2026-05.md` → v0.26.2.

# v0.26.1 — wire skills discovery into the central prompt

A small follow-up to v0.26.0 that makes the new capability-routing skill actually reachable by the model.

## What changed

- **Central prompt rule 7.** `UnrealMcpAssistantSystemPromptBuilder` now tells every server-message provider: *before scaffolding a new tool or productizing a completed workflow, FIRST consult project skills via `unreal.skill_list` / `unreal.skill_read` (start with `mcp-capability-routing`); a direct "make a tool" request uses the Python user-extension track, never a handler hand-merged into core.* v0.26.0 shipped the skill but never instructed the model to read it — this closes that gap.
- **`mcp-capability-routing` skill** (shipped in 524bda5, included here): a front-door router. "Do X" → find/compose existing tools via `tool_recommend` / `tool_gap_analyze`; "make a tool" → the safe Python user-extension track (scaffold → reload → smoke), never a core-merge. Framed around the actual v0.26 incident: a direct request to make a tool was legitimate — the fault was the build *path*, not the decision to build.

## Compatibility

- **No tool-surface change** — registry stays **162**. `EAiProviderKind` unchanged.
- Dual-engine: builds + **48/48 automation PASS** on both UE 5.6 and UE 5.7 (`UnrealMcp.AssistantSystemPromptBuilder` now asserts all 7 rules).
- Additive prompt rule only; existing behavior preserved.

## Verify

```
# macOS
shasum -a 256 -c UnrealMcp-v0.26.1-mac-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip.sha256
# expected: 949718b213ffabbbbe51d4cafb4d8c629540e9889e4145f5c1cfb690881607c1

# Windows (PowerShell)
Get-FileHash UnrealMcp-v0.26.1-win-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip -Algorithm SHA256
```

#### Release Body

# v0.26.0 — Reform C (extension safety: approval gate + Python user-extension track + lifecycle)

Closes the 7 root causes (RC-1..RC-7) behind the v0.25→v0.26 incident, where in-editor AI followed the documented scaffold workflow and merged a runtime-broken 291-line embedded-Python C++ handler into core plugin source — silently bumping the tool count, hanging `mcp_tool_audit`, and crashing the editor on shutdown (`Py_FinalizeEx` SEGV). Reform C makes AI self-extension **safe by construction**: an approval gate, a first-class Python user-extension track that never touches core, a lifecycle contract that prevents premature "it works" claims, and a central safety prompt that can no longer be empty.

## What changed

### 1. Central system-prompt builder — 6 safety rules, never empty (RC-1)

All three server-message providers (`OpenAiResponses` via AssistantRun, `OpenAiChatCompat`, `AnthropicMessages`) now share `UnrealMcpAssistantSystemPromptBuilder`. The 6 Reform C safety rules are **baked in** — they appear even when the user's `AssistantSystemPrompt` setting is empty (the exact condition that left the incident model unguarded). The user's optional prompt is appended after the rules; per-provider steering paths are preserved unchanged.

The 6 rules, in brief:
1. Don't claim a tool is callable until `lifecycle.callableNow=true` AND smoke/audit confirms.
2. User Python tools: scaffold → reload → smoke → then call.
3. Core C++ tools: dry-run → apply → build → restart → audit → then call.
4. On `approval_required` / `requiresApproval=true`: stop and wait for human approval.
5. Never turn a `dryRun` result into a success claim.
6. Write-capable user tools default to `dryRun=true` + return `wouldWrite` first.

### 2. Approval gate at the AssistantRun seam (RC-4, RC-6)

High-risk tool calls (real `mcp_apply_scaffold`, core writes, build/restart) now pause for explicit user approval **before** execution. The gate lives at the AssistantRun seam — NOT the global dispatcher — so external MCP / CLI / Codex-bridge callers keep working unchanged. The ChatPanel surfaces an inline approval card; approve resumes the deferred call, reject blocks it.

### 3. Python user-extension track is now the default (RC-2, RC-3, RC-7)

`unreal.scaffold_mcp_tool` now defaults to `implementationTrack=python` and generates a single-file project-local tool at `Tools/UnrealMcpPyTools/<tool_id>/main.py` — **zero `*.patch.cpp`, zero core mutation**. The legacy C++ core track still exists but is now "core developer mode" gated behind approval. Two new control tools manage the hot lifecycle:

- `unreal.mcp_user_registry_reload` — rescans the project-local Python tools, sha256-validates `main.py`, hot-reloads via `main.py` reimport (no dylib hot-swap, no restart). Reports added/updated/removed/rejected counts.
- `unreal.mcp_user_tool_smoke` — invokes a freshly-loaded user tool under a bounded timeout; only after `smoke_passed` may the assistant claim it works.

A user-tool lock serializes reload-vs-execute and same-tool concurrent execution. **Windows-supported from day one** (uses UE PythonScriptPlugin, no shell/subprocess).

### 4. Lifecycle contract + audit taxonomy clarity (RC-5)

Every scaffold/apply/reload/smoke/audit result now carries an additive `structuredContent.lifecycle` object (state machine + `callableNow` + `nextRequiredAction` + sourceKind/handlerKind + derived flags). `mcp_tool_audit` is now explicit that it is **static** (`auditMode=static_registry_and_handler_reconciliation`, `didInvokeHandlers=false`) and reports an 11-code issue taxonomy — clearing the confusion that made the incident audit look like it "hung on a handler".

## Tool surface

160 → **162** canonical core tools (the 2 new control tools). User Python tools do **not** bump the canonical count — they live in a separate project-local overlay registry. `EAiProviderKind` unchanged (append-only preserved).

## Compatibility

- **Dual-engine**: builds + 48/48 automation tests PASS on **both UE 5.6 and UE 5.7** (Mac).
- **Backward-compatible**: all existing tool result fields preserved; `lifecycle` is additive. External MCP/CLI clients that ignore it keep working.
- **Codex CLI + Codex Desktop providers**: unchanged this release (they own their own prompt assembly via external process; central-builder integration is a v0.27 follow-up — noted in `Docs/AIProviderArchitecture.md`).

## Verify

```
# macOS
shasum -a 256 -c UnrealMcp-v0.26.0-mac-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip.sha256
# expected: aefd70b166d696b237e20664181d887ac29ce00bc6e9a57fee91fd7634a8dc81

# Windows (PowerShell)
Get-FileHash UnrealMcp-v0.26.0-win-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip -Algorithm SHA256
# expected: 358088810d7821776ed0b8c2862e5de85a58e34f5052987e5cea94e9a5b43fac
```

> Both zips are source-only project-root packages for UE 5.6/5.7. The Windows zip is built + verified by the `Windows Release Package` CI workflow on `windows-2022` and attached here.

Full trilingual notes (中文 / EN / 日本語): `Docs/Release-2026-05.md` → v0.26.0 section.
Architecture + RC-1..RC-7 resolution: `Docs/AIProviderArchitecture.md`.

#### Release Body

# v0.25.0 — Reform B (Codex CLI exec rewrite)

Resolves the v0.24.4 Known Limitations **G1** (Codex CLI provider chat didn't return the assistant reply to the UE Assistant panel) and **G4** (composed-prompt argv length risk). Codex CLI provider now actually works for chat round-trip on Mac/Linux.

## Breaking change for Codex CLI provider users

`Codex Binary Path` setting must change from `…/codex-orchestrator/bin/codex-agent` to the **`codex` CLI binary** directly. v0.25 replaced the codex-agent wrapper with direct `codex exec` invocation.

### Migration (5 steps)

1. Install or locate codex CLI:
   ```
   which codex
   # → typical: /opt/homebrew/bin/codex (Apple Silicon Homebrew)
   # → typical: /usr/local/bin/codex (Intel Homebrew)
   ```
2. In `Project Settings → Plugins → Unreal MCP → AI → Providers`, update the Codex CLI provider entry's **Codex Binary Path** to the path from step 1.
3. **Remove** `-m gpt-5.5 -r xhigh` from **Codex Extra Args** (or rewrite using codex CLI `-c key="value"` syntax: `-c reasoning_effort="high"`). v0.25 rejects `-r`/`--reasoning` because `codex exec` doesn't accept them. Baseline flags (`model`, `sandbox_mode`, `reasoning_effort`) are auto-injected.
4. Run `codex login` in a terminal (first time only — codex CLI requires OAuth).
5. Smoke-test UEAtelier Chat by selecting the Codex CLI provider in the chat panel and sending "test".

The migration error messages in v0.25 are explicit about what to change — you'll see a clear instruction if the old `codex-agent` path or `-r` flag is detected during ValidateConfig.

## What this fixes (G1)

### Root cause

`codex-agent start -w` waited for job `status != running`, but upstream `codex` CLI is **interactive**:
- processes the first prompt
- replies
- then sits idle forever waiting for the next user input — never exits

The UE chat pump on the parent `/bin/bash` stdout only ever saw codex-agent's `"Job started: <uuid>"` header. Codex's actual reply lived in a tmux pane that the parent process never read. v0.24.4 fixed 3 bash-quoting bugs in the pipeline but left this architectural gap.

### Approach (Path A)

Invoke `codex` CLI binary directly via:
```bash
bash -c "PATH=...&& codex exec --json --ephemeral --skip-git-repo-check \
  -C <projdir> \
  -c model='\"gpt-5.5\"' \
  -c reasoning_effort='\"xhigh\"' \
  -c sandbox_mode='\"workspace-write\"' \
  <user extras> <user prompt>"
```

- **3 pipes** (stdin + stdout + stderr) via `FPlatformProcess::CreateProc`
- **ConversationContext** is passed via the child subprocess's **stdin pipe** (closed after write to signal EOF) — resolves G4 (no more argv length cap)
- **JSONL stdout** is parsed line-by-line (`TJsonReaderFactory<TCHAR>` per complete `\n`-bounded line, with incremental buffering for partial lines split across `ReadPipe` boundaries)
- **`item.completed`** with `agent_message` → `TextDelta` event to UI
- **Stderr** is buffered for auth-failure detection
- **401 Unauthorized** / **Missing bearer** / **Reconnecting** → single friendly "Run `codex login`" event (rate-limited per FCodexRun to suppress reconnect spam)
- **Cancellation** = `FPlatformProcess::TerminateProc(handle, /*killTree=*/true)` — SIGTERM cascades to codex CLI via process tree

## Dependencies removed for the Codex CLI provider

- ~~codex-agent~~ (no longer required — direct codex CLI invocation)
- ~~bun~~ (codex-agent was the only Bun consumer)
- ~~tmux~~ (no more interactive tmux session juggling)

## What stays untouched

**Codex Desktop / App Server bridge** is **byte-identical** pre/post. Different provider (`CodexAppServer`), different transport (WebSocket), different file (`CodexAppServerProvider.{h,cpp}`). v0.25's codex dispatch verified `git diff` returns empty for those files + `IAssistantProvider.h`. Codex Desktop users see zero impact; both providers coexist in Settings UI.

All non-Codex-CLI providers (`OpenAiResponses` / `OpenAiChatCompletions` / `AnthropicMessages`) untouched. `EAiProviderKind` append-only preserved. **160-tool registry** unchanged.

## Section B invariants (now 10)

`Docs/AIProviderArchitecture.md` Section B documents the full set of shell-escaping + subprocess invariants:

1. Exactly 1 literal ASCII space in `Arguments` string (the `-c <command>` separator)
2. 0 literal ASCII double-quote characters
3. Trusted generated shell fragments may contain `=`, `$HOME`, `$PATH`, `${IFS}`, `&&`, `$'...'`
4. User/config-derived values never concatenated raw
5. User/config-derived values only as output of `QuoteForBashWordNoSpaces` or rejected upstream
6. Command parts joined with `${IFS}`, never literal ASCII space
7. No `"..."` wrapping, `"$(cat ...)"` substitution, or any construct introducing literal `"`
8. PATH augmentation uses bare `PATH=…&&${IFS}<cmd>` (NOT `export PATH=…&&…`) — avoids word-split when inherited `$PATH` contains `/Library/Application Support/...`
9. **NEW**: `ConversationContext` for multi-turn chat passed via child stdin pipe (closed after write), NOT argv
10. **NEW**: Cancellation uses `TerminateProc(handle, /*killTree=*/true)` directly, not separate `kill <jobId>` subprocess

## Known limitation (NOT fixed in v0.25 — tracked as v0.26+ candidates)

- **G6 (NEW)**: codex exec emits `agent_message` as **one complete** `item.completed` event, not token-level deltas. UE chat shows the full reply atomically (no incremental token streaming). Future enhancement could investigate codex's streaming config if any.
- G2: tilde (`~`) not expanded in `CodexBinaryPath` (user must enter absolute path)
- G3: hardcoded subprocess PATH augmentation list (5 dirs, no override setting)
- G5: provider observability uneven (no structured telemetry)

## Compatibility / Scope

- **Codex CLI provider only** (`EAiProviderKind::Codex`). Codex Desktop (`CodexAppServer`) untouched.
- **Mac/Linux only**. Codex CLI provider's `ValidateCodexConfig` returns false on `PLATFORM_WINDOWS`; Windows users continue using Codex Desktop bridge.
- v0.24.0 through v0.24.4 user-visible behavior preserved EXCEPT Codex CLI provider chat (now actually works).
- Registry remains **160 MCP tools** across 11 categories.

## Validation

- `python3 Tools/check_ue56_compat.py` → 0 errors, 0 warnings (min engine 5.6)
- `python3 Tools/validate_tool_registry.py` → 160 tools, mirrorToolCount 160, issueCount 0
- `git diff --check` → clean
- UE 5.6 Mac MyProjectEditor build → exit 0, 49.5s clean
- UE 5.7 Mac MyProjectEditor build → exit 0, 5.79s incremental (post-enum-fix)
- UE 5.6 + UE 5.7 × 11 automation tests = **22 runs, all PASS**:
  - **6 NEW CodexProvider tests**: SubprocessPathPrefix, ExecCommandBuild, JsonlEventParser, AuthDetection, MigrationPredicates, ExecCommandActualBashExec (integration)
  - 4 ProviderPresets regressions: RegistryAndApply, NestedChainEvent, IntlPresetURLs, LegacyOpenAIMigration
  - 1 ChatCompat regression: QuirkHandlers

The new `ExecCommandActualBashExec` integration test exec's a fake codex script (hardcoded GUID'd argv/stdin paths) through real `/bin/bash -c`, asserts: argv has `exec --json --ephemeral --skip-git-repo-check` + `-C <projdir>` + 3 baseline `-c` flags + user prompt LAST + no `ConversationContext` in argv; stdin file exact bytes match `ConversationContext`; JSONL parser correctly reassembles an event split across 2 writes (partial-line buffering coverage).

## Install

Extract the projectroot zip next to your `<YourProject>.uproject`. Same source compiles cleanly on UE 5.6 and UE 5.7.

## Workflow

6-round PM↔Hermes schema-lock + PM ship-time enum fix:

- **R1** (PM brief → Hermes critique): 13 architectural catches including stderr pipe necessity, JSONL parser approach, `-m` accepted vs `-r` rejected, auth detection, fake script approach
- **R2** (PM frozen schema + 12 asks → Hermes critique): 5 schema deltas (command argument order, worker-thread chunked stdin, hardcoded GUID test paths, ValidateConfig testability, codex config key verification) + 3 clarifications
- **R3** (PM codex prompt + 24-item red-team → Hermes red-team): 1 blocker (R3 prompt contained imperative `git rm` command violating SCOPE GUARDS)
- **R5** (after R4 git rm fix → Hermes red-team + dispatch + capture): PROMPT_OK; codex dispatched, ran 18m32s, 11-file scope exact match, CodexAppServer + IAssistantProvider isolation EMPTY diff
- **R6** (Hermes build+test): blocked by safety layer on `rm -rf`; PM took over
- **PM ship-time**: 1 enum value bug (`EUnrealMcpAssistantEventType::Error` doesn't exist — only Status/TextDelta/ToolCallStarted/ToolCallFinished); PM inline-fixed 3 sites to use `Status` + explicit error-text prefix; UE 5.7 incremental rebuild + UE 5.6 clean rebuild + 22/22 automation matrix all PASS

- `UnrealMcp-v0.25.0-mac-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip` (Mac, PM manual upload)
- `UnrealMcp-v0.25.0-win-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip` (Win, GitHub Actions on tag push, PM downloads + attaches)

#### Release Body

# v0.24.4 — Codex CLI bash-quoting hotfix (3 bugs) + Provider Architecture invariants

Fixes three bash-quoting bugs in CodexProvider that broke Codex CLI provider chat (v0.24.3 regression + pre-existing latent bug + ship-time-discovered bug caught by the NEW integration tests this release introduces). Adds the first written record of Provider-layer architectural invariants (`Docs/AIProviderArchitecture.md`, 8 invariants in Section B).

## What this fixes

### Bug 1 — v0.24.3 regression: literal `"..."` in PATH wrapper

v0.24.3 added a dev-tool PATH augmentation prefix in `GetCodexSubprocessPathPrefix()`:

```cpp
"export${IFS}PATH=\"$HOME/.bun/bin:...:$PATH\"&&${IFS}"
```

The two `\"` characters violated a CodexProvider design invariant: the `Arguments` string passed to `FPlatformProcess::CreateProc` must contain **zero literal `"` characters**. The UE Unix CreateProc tokenizer (`ParseCmdLineToken` in `UnixPlatformProcess.cpp`) treats `"` as a quote delimiter and captures double-double-quoted text into argv. Result at runtime: `bash: -c: option requires an argument`.

**Fix**: removed the redundant `"..."` wrapping. POSIX bash assignment RHS is not word-split anyway, so the quoting was defensive against a non-issue and cost the entire chat flow.

### Bug 2 — Pre-v0.24.3 latent: literal `"$(cat...)"` in prompt-pass

`CodexProvider.cpp:577` (pre-existing for months) used:

```cpp
CommandParts.Add(FString::Printf(TEXT("\"$(cat${IFS}%s)\""), *Quoted(PromptTempFilePath)));
```

Same tokenizer quirk eats the outer `"..."`. Was masked by `bun: not found` failing earlier in the pipeline. v0.24.3 PATH fix unmasked it: chat got past `bash: -c` but hit `Error: No prompt provided` from codex-agent receiving mangled argv.

**Fix**: pass the composed prompt text directly as a single `$'...'`-wrapped argv word via existing `QuoteForBashWordNoSpaces` helper. Multi-turn `ConversationContext` is preserved (the helper accepts `ComposePrompt(UserPrompt, ConversationContext)` output, not raw `UserPrompt`).

### Bug 3 — Ship-time: `export VAR=value` word-splits inherited $PATH

After Bug 1's fix, the form `export${IFS}PATH=...:$PATH&&${IFS}` exposed a NEW class of failure caught by the new integration tests this release introduces (this is what they were designed for).

Root cause: `export VAR=value` is the export BUILTIN. POSIX bash word-splits the builtin's single argument (`VAR=value`) after parameter expansion. When inherited `$PATH` contains directories with literal spaces — universal on macOS via paths like `/Library/Application Support/JetBrains/Toolbox/scripts` — the expanded assignment splits at the space and `export` receives multiple args. The second arg is not a valid identifier:

```
/bin/bash: line 0: export: `Support/JetBrains/Toolbox/scripts:...:/Library/Application': not a valid identifier
```

**Fix**: change `export${IFS}PATH=...&&${IFS}` to `PATH=...&&${IFS}`. The bare `PATH=value` form (no `export` keyword) is a current-shell variable assignment whose RHS is POSIX-guaranteed NOT word-split post-expansion. `$PATH` is already exported by the parent UE Editor process, so re-assignment preserves the exported status and the new value propagates to child processes via standard env inheritance.

**Documented as invariant #8 in `Docs/AIProviderArchitecture.md` Section B.**

This bug would have shipped silently to all Mac users (`/Library/Application Support/...` is on basically every macOS install) without the new integration tests. The integration tests caught it on the first PM-side run and the fix took 1 line + 1 comment.

## What changed (7 files, 906 insertions / 94 deletions)

### Production code

- **`CodexProvider.cpp`** (+296/-95): Edit A fixes the EnvPrefix (Bugs 1 + 3 combined into the final `PATH=...` form), Edit B fixes the prompt-pass (Bug 2), Edit C adds defensive `\x22` encoding for `"` inside `QuoteForBashWordNoSpaces`, Edits D-E move `QuoteForBashWordNoSpaces` / `JoinShellArgumentsNoSpaces` / `ComposePrompt` from anonymous namespace into `UnrealMcp::Providers::Internal` and extract `BuildCodexStartCommand()` / `BuildCodexKillCommand()` production helpers exercised by both production code AND the new integration tests, Edit F adds a file-top invariant comment authoritatively mirroring `Docs/AIProviderArchitecture.md` Section B's 8 invariants verbatim.
- **`CodexProviderShellHelpers.h`** (+44 new): minimal private header exposing the 5 helpers to tests. Lives at `Private/Providers/` so module include convention `#include "Providers/CodexProviderShellHelpers.h"` applies.

### Tests

- **`UnrealMcpProviderPresetTests.cpp`** (+255/-1): updated existing `SubprocessPathPrefix` assertion (no trailing `\"`, plus `StartsWith("PATH=")` + `!Contains("export")` for Bug 3); added two NEW integration tests `SpawnedCommandActualBashExec` + `KillCommandActualBashExec` that exec the actual production-built command through `/bin/bash -c` against a deterministic argc/argv-printing helper script. Both assert: exit code 0, exactly 1 literal ASCII space in `Arguments`, zero literal `"` in `Arguments`, and the composed prompt arrives intact as ONE argv slot through bash `-c` round-trip — including embedded spaces, quotes, newlines, tabs.

### Documentation

- **`Docs/AIProviderArchitecture.md`** (+294 new, EN only): first written record of Provider-layer architectural invariants. Sections A (5-kind × 3-transport taxonomy) / **B (CodexProvider shell-escaping — 8 invariants, the critical section)** / C (Settings UI patterns) / D (region awareness gap) / E (testing strategy — why pure-string tests aren't sufficient) / F (known UE gotchas) / G (5 known limitations: G1=Codex CLI interactive mismatch, G2=tilde expansion, G3=hardcoded PATH list, G4=composed-prompt argv length, G5=provider observability).
- **`Docs/Release-2026-05.md`** (+105/-0): trilingual v0.24.4 entry (中/EN/日).
- **`AGENTS.md`** (+1/-1): VersionName bump 0.24.3 → 0.24.4 (no other Freshness threshold crossed).
- **`UnrealMcp.uplugin`** (+2/-2): Version 33→34, VersionName 0.24.3→0.24.4.

## Known limitation (NOT fixed in v0.24.4 — tracked as v0.25 Reform B candidate G1)

Even after these fixes, **Codex CLI provider chat through the UE Assistant panel still does NOT return codex's reply** to the chat UI. Root cause is architectural, not a quoting bug:

- `codex-agent start -w` waits for job `status != running`
- `codex` CLI is interactive: processes the first prompt, replies, then **sits idle forever waiting for the next user input** — `-w` never returns
- The UE chat pump on the parent `/bin/bash` stdout only ever sees codex-agent's `"Job started: <uuid>"` header
- Codex's actual reply lives in a tmux pane that the parent process never reads

**Workaround (works today)**: Use the **Codex Desktop bridge** (`CodexAppServer` provider, WebSocket to local Codex Desktop). PM-validated, no changes needed.

**Fix path (v0.25 Reform B)**: Rewrite `SpawnProcess` to use `codex exec <prompt>` (one-shot mode) OR `codex-agent start ... + await-turn + capture` pattern. See `Docs/AIProviderArchitecture.md` Section G (G1).

The v0.24.4 fixes still ship value: any non-interactive scripting / inspection of the bash command no longer breaks at the CreateProc tokenizer layer NOR at the `export $PATH` word-split layer.

## Compatibility / Scope

- **Codex CLI provider only** (`EAiProviderKind::Codex`). Codex Desktop (`CodexAppServer`) untouched.
- **Mac/Linux only**. Codex CLI provider's `ValidateCodexConfig` returns false on `PLATFORM_WINDOWS`; Windows users continue using Codex Desktop bridge.
- No INI / settings change. Existing user `Codex Binary Path` preserved.
- No `EAiProviderKind` enum change (append-only project rule).
- No 10-preset registry change.
- Other providers (`OpenAiResponses` / `OpenAiChatCompletions` / `AnthropicMessages` / `CodexAppServer`) untouched.
- v0.24.0 through v0.24.3 behavior preserved (with Bugs 1 + 3 fixed).
- Registry remains **160 MCP tools** across 11 categories.

#### Release Body

# v0.24.3 — Codex CLI subprocess PATH augmentation

Fixes `bun: not found` (and similar PATH-resolution failures) when invoking Codex CLI provider from in-editor chat.

## What this fixes

When UE Editor launches Codex CLI subprocess, it inherits the minimal macOS default PATH (`/usr/bin:/bin:/usr/sbin:/sbin`) and does NOT source the user's `.zshrc` / `.bash_profile`. The codex-agent shell script's line 10 — `exec bun "$SCRIPT_DIR/../src/cli.ts" "$@"` — uses bare `bun`, which fails because Bun is typically installed at `$HOME/.bun/bin/bun` (not in default PATH).

User-reported error:
```
/Users/<user>/codex-orchestrator/bin/codex-agent: line 10: exec: bun: not found
Codex process exited with code 127.
```

## What changed (plugin-side fix only — codex-orchestrator install untouched)

**`CodexProvider.cpp`** now prepends a `PATH` export to the `bash -c` command before invoking codex-agent. Augmented PATH covers 5 common Mac developer tool directories:

| Path | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `$HOME/.bun/bin` | Bun (Codex Orchestrator dependency) — the actual user fix |
| `$HOME/.local/bin` | pip user installs, manual binaries |
| `$HOME/.cargo/bin` | Rust cargo |
| `/opt/homebrew/bin` | Homebrew on Apple Silicon Macs |
| `/usr/local/bin` | Homebrew on Intel Macs, manual /usr/local installs |

Shell silently ignores non-existent entries — no harm if a user doesn't have a particular dir.

## Implementation details

- New helper `UnrealMcp::Providers::GetCodexSubprocessPathPrefix()` returns the IFS-safe `export${IFS}PATH="..."&&${IFS}` prefix. Non-static free function in `CodexProvider.cpp` (no header change — Option C1 layout per Hermes R2).
- **IFS-safe** (no literal ASCII spaces in command fragment) so UE `CreateProc` parameter parsing through `bash -c` doesn't split on whitespace. Matches existing `${IFS}` discipline at the joined `CommandParts` site.
- **Two exec sites updated**:
  1. **Main chat exec** (line ~588): `Command = GetCodexSubprocessPathPrefix() + FString::Join(CommandParts, "${IFS}")`
  2. **Cancel/kill exec** (lines 662-688): full restructure from direct `CreateProc(Codex binary, "kill JobId")` to `CreateProc("/bin/bash", "-c <prefix>${IFS}<binary>${IFS}kill${IFS}<jobId>")`, so PATH augmentation also covers the cleanup path. JobId is `QuoteForBashWordNoSpaces`'d for symmetry even though `LooksLikeJobId` already restricts captured IDs to alnum / `-` / `_`.

## Compatibility / Scope

- **Codex CLI provider only** (`EAiProviderKind::Codex`). Codex Desktop (`CodexAppServer`) is unchanged — it uses `IWebSocket`, no subprocess.
- **Mac/Linux only**. Codex CLI provider's `ValidateCodexConfig` returns false on `PLATFORM_WINDOWS`, so the new prefix is never reached on Windows. Windows users continue using Codex Desktop bridge.
- No INI / settings change. Existing user `Codex Binary Path` preserved.
- No `EAiProviderKind` enum change (append-only project rule)
- No 10-preset registry change
- Other providers (`OpenAiResponses` / `OpenAiChatCompletions` / `AnthropicMessages`) untouched
- Phase 1 + Phase 2 + v0.24.1 + v0.24.2 behavior preserved
- Registry remains **160 MCP tools** across 11 categories
- No header change — helper is in `UnrealMcp::Providers` namespace in `CodexProvider.cpp`; test forward-declares it (Option C1)

## Validation (all PASS)

- `python3 Tools/check_ue56_compat.py` → 0 errors, 0 warnings
- `python3 Tools/validate_tool_registry.py` → 160 tools, matched=50, issueCount=0
- `git diff --check` → clean
- UE 5.6 Mac MyProjectEditor build → exit 0, 20.77s fresh
- UE 5.7 Mac MyProjectEditor build → exit 0, 17.95s fresh
- UE 5.6 + UE 5.7 × 6 automation tests = **12 runs, all Success**:
  - `ProviderPresets.RegistryAndApply` (regression)
  - `ProviderPresets.NestedChainEvent` (v0.24.1 regression)
  - `ProviderPresets.IntlPresetURLs` (v0.24.2 regression)
  - `ProviderPresets.LegacyOpenAIMigration` (v0.24.2 regression)
  - `ChatCompat.QuirkHandlers` (Phase 2 regression)
  - **`CodexProvider.SubprocessPathPrefix` (NEW)** — 8 assertions: 5 path substrings + ends with `:$PATH"&&${IFS}` + non-empty + zero literal ASCII space

## Install

Extract the projectroot zip next to your `<YourProject>.uproject`. Same source compiles cleanly on UE 5.6 and UE 5.7. Codex CLI users on Mac no longer need to manually edit codex-agent script after every codex-orchestrator update.

# v0.24.2 — Hide deprecated UI + intl-first preset URLs

Two UX fixes for users outside mainland China (default reasonable for Tokyo / EU / US / etc.):

## What this fixes

1. **Hide 4 deprecated `Open AI*` legacy fields** from Project Settings → Plugins → UEAtelier → AI panel. These pre-`Providers[]` global fields (`Open AIResponses Url` / `Open AIApi Key` / `Open AIModel` / `Open AIReasoning Effort`) were marked `DeprecatedProperty` but UE Property Editor doesn't honor that marker — they still rendered, causing "which field do I fill?" confusion.

2. **Flip 3 vendor preset BaseUrl defaults to international endpoints** (intl-first per non-CN users):

| Preset | v0.24.1 default (CN) | v0.24.2 default (intl) |
|---|---|---|
| **Kimi (Moonshot)** | `api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions` | `api.moonshot.ai/v1/chat/completions` |
| **GLM (Zhipu)** | `open.bigmodel.cn/api/paas/v4/chat/completions` | `api.z.ai/api/paas/v4/chat/completions` (Zhipu's intl rebrand "Z.ai") |
| **Qwen (Tongyi)** | `dashscope.aliyuncs.com/compatible-mode/...` | `dashscope-intl.aliyuncs.com/compatible-mode/...` |

DeepSeek / Ollama / OpenAI / Anthropic / Codex unchanged (already intl or region-agnostic).

## Upgrade notes — existing user configs preserved

**No automatic INI migration.** If you upgraded from v0.24.0 / v0.24.1 and already have a `kimi` (or `glm`/`qwen`) provider entry with `BaseUrl="...cn..."`, your saved BaseUrl is preserved — you may be a deliberate CN user.

**To switch to intl on existing entry**:
- (a) Clear the BaseUrl field and re-pick PresetId to the same value → v0.24.2's `PostEditChangeChainProperty` (added in v0.24.1) overwrites with new intl URL
- (b) OR manually edit BaseUrl in Project Settings to the new URL

**New users picking preset after v0.24.2** get intl URLs automatically.

## Mainland China users

If you're in mainland CN and the intl endpoint is slow/blocked, you can manually edit BaseUrl back to the `.cn` variant after picking the preset. The preset registry no longer ships CN URLs as defaults, but the dispatcher supports any URL the OpenAI-compatible endpoint follows.

## Technical changes

- `UnrealMcpSettings.h`: 4 deprecated UPROPERTYs lose `EditAnywhere` (keep `Config` for INI load + migration). 1 new helper declaration.
- `UnrealMcpSettings.cpp`: Migration body refactored into `ApplyLegacyOpenAIMigration_IfNeeded()` helper. Called by both `PostInitProperties()` and the new automation test (avoids UObject thread-context poisoning from direct `PostInitProperties()` re-invocation).
- `UnrealMcpProviderPresets.cpp`: 3 URL flips in the 10-preset hardcoded list.
- 2 new automation tests:
  - `UnrealMcp.ProviderPresets.IntlPresetURLs` — verifies all 3 intl URLs + defensive "no `.cn` URL in registry" assertion
  - `UnrealMcp.ProviderPresets.LegacyOpenAIMigration` — verifies migration helper preserves legacy ApiKey/BaseUrl/Model/Effort
- `RegistryAndApply` existing test: 3 URL assertions updated to match new defaults.

## Validation (all PASS)

- `python3 Tools/check_ue56_compat.py` → 0 errors, 0 warnings
- `python3 Tools/validate_tool_registry.py` → 160 tools, matched=50, issueCount=0
- `git diff --check` → clean
- UE 5.6 Mac MyProjectEditor build → exit 0, 18.96s fresh
- UE 5.7 Mac MyProjectEditor build → exit 0, 17.58s fresh
- UE 5.6 + UE 5.7 × 5 automation tests = **10 runs, all Success**:
  - `ProviderPresets.RegistryAndApply` (regression with updated URL assertions)

#### Release Body

# v0.24.1 — Fix nested Provider preset auto-fill

Hotfix for the v0.24.0 Phase 1 AI Provider Preset System: picking `PresetId` (or changing `Kind`) in Project Settings → Plugins → UEAtelier → AI → Providers now correctly auto-fills `BaseUrl` / `Model` / `DisplayName`.

## What this fixes

User reported that picking `Preset Id = "kimi"` saved `PresetId` to INI but left `BaseUrl` and `Model` empty.

**Root cause** (UE 5.6 + 5.7 engine-source-cited):
- Nested `Providers[]` property changes route through `UObject::PostEditChangeChainProperty`
- The default UObject impl forwards to `PostEditChangeProperty` but the forwarded event loses the `Providers` array index
- Our settings class only overrode `PostEditChangeProperty` (Phase 1 design oversight against the wrong UE callback path)
- `GetArrayIndex("Providers")` returned -1, our auto-fill branches silently no-op'd

This also explains why the existing v0.20 `Kind` auto-fill (commit `370a2ab`) never actually fired in the UI either — silent regression that no test caught.

## What changed

- `UUnrealMcpSettings` now overrides `PostEditChangeChainProperty` and routes through a shared helper `TryApplyPresetForProviderChange()`
- Helper covers BOTH `PresetId` (ExplicitPresetSelection) AND `Kind` (FillEmpty with OpenAiChatCompat placeholder preserved)
- Backup trigger is now event-based via `IsProvidersChangeEvent` predicate (runs for any provider-related change, not gated on preset apply success)
- New automation test `UnrealMcp.ProviderPresets.NestedChainEvent` covers 4 regression axes (PresetId chain event, Kind chain event, invalid array index, non-target leaf no-op)
- Plugin metadata bumped: `Version: 30 → 31`, `VersionName: 0.24.0 → 0.24.1`

## Compatibility

- `EAiProviderKind` unchanged (append-only project rule)
- `FAiProviderConfig` struct unchanged
- 10-preset registry unchanged
- All provider runtime dispatchers unchanged
- Phase 1 + Phase 2 behavior preserved
- Registry remains 160 MCP tools across 11 categories

## Validation (all PASS)

- `python3 Tools/check_ue56_compat.py` → 0 errors, 0 warnings
- `python3 Tools/validate_tool_registry.py` → 160 tools, matched=50, issueCount=0
- `git diff --check` → clean
- UE 5.6 Mac MyProjectEditor build → exit 0, 25.13s fresh
- UE 5.7 Mac MyProjectEditor build → exit 0, 18.38s fresh
- UE 5.6 `UnrealMcp.ProviderPresets.RegistryAndApply` automation → Success (regression)
- UE 5.6 `UnrealMcp.ProviderPresets.NestedChainEvent` automation → Success (NEW)
- UE 5.6 `UnrealMcp.ChatCompat.QuirkHandlers` automation → Success (regression)
- UE 5.7 `UnrealMcp.ProviderPresets.RegistryAndApply` automation → Success (regression)
- UE 5.7 `UnrealMcp.ProviderPresets.NestedChainEvent` automation → Success (NEW)
- UE 5.7 `UnrealMcp.ChatCompat.QuirkHandlers` automation → Success (regression)

#### Release Body

## v0.23.1 — CLI-only hotfix

This is a **CLI-only release**. The Unreal plugin (`Plugins/UnrealMcp/`) is unchanged from v0.23.0 — no need to re-extract or rebuild. No plugin zip is attached to this release.

### What changed

**1. `status` command now returns a richer payload.** Three fields added, sourced from `unreal.editor_status`:
- `projectName`
- `currentMap`
- `isPlayInEditor`

Fields are **omitted** (not `null`) when `editor_status` is unavailable, keeping the JSON schema strictly additive.

New JSON shape (all 7 fields):
```json
{
  "endpoint": "http://127.0.0.1:8765/mcp",
  "connected": true,
  "editorVersion": "5.7.4",
  "toolCount": 160,
  "projectName": "MyProject",
  "currentMap": "/Game/Maps/Main",
  "isPlayInEditor": false
}
```

**2. Fixed a latent bug shipping since v0.23.0.** When `editor_status` was unavailable, the `editor.engine_version` fallback **always returned `"unknown"`** because the alias table didn't recognize the `version_string` key the C++ tool emits. The test fake masked it with a synthetic `unrealVersion` field. Alias table now accepts `version_string`.

**3. Fallback chain (locked):**
- `editor_status` succeeds → full 7-field payload
- `editor_status` returns `isError=true` → fall back to `editor.engine_version` (3 new fields omitted)
- `editor.engine_version` also `isError=true` → `editorVersion: "unknown"` (3 new fields omitted)
- Client/protocol errors (endpoint unreachable / HTTP error / JSON-RPC error) **re-raise** with their existing exit codes (2/4/3); never fall back

### Install / upgrade

```bash
pip install --upgrade "git+https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEAtelier.git@v0.23.1#subdirectory=Tools/UEAtelierCli"
```

### Test coverage

5 status tests cover the matrix: success / isError fallback / both-isError / mid-call EndpointUnreachable / empty currentMap omission. Total CLI test suite: **22/22 green**.

`FakeClient` extended to support per-call exceptions (backward-compatible with existing dict/list response fixtures).

### No plugin changes

- `Plugins/UnrealMcp/UnrealMcp.uplugin` `VersionName` stays `0.23.0`
- Registry: 160 tools (unchanged)
- No C++ changes
- No `AGENTS.md` change required (freshness clause evaluated)

### Process notes

Designed via 3-round Hermes coordinator review:
- Round 1 critique caught the latent `version_string` bug (PM's residual-fix scope grew to include it)
- Round 2 NOT-PROMPT_OK with 4 schema-rule revisions (exception class taxonomy, double-gating, test matrix count, FakeClient extension API)
- Round 3 PROMPT_OK after patches; dispatched `codex-agent` with `-m gpt-5.5 -r xhigh -s workspace-write`

Co-authored:
- Codex (gpt-5.5, xhigh)
- Claude Opus 4.7 (1M context)

#### Release Body

## What's New

`cli-anything-ueatelier` — a pip-installable Python CLI that lets any agent (not just MCP-aware ones) drive UEAtelier from the shell. Submitted for inclusion in the [HKUDS/CLI-Anything](https://github.com/HKUDS/CLI-Anything) Hub.

**No new MCP tools.** Registry stays at 160. The CLI is a CONSUMER, not a producer.

### Install

```bash
pip install git+https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEAtelier.git#subdirectory=Tools/UEAtelierCli
```

Then with Unreal Editor + UEAtelier plugin running:

```bash
cli-anything-ueatelier status
cli-anything-ueatelier diagnostics --classes log_error,log_warning --limit 20
cli-anything-ueatelier pie-smoke --map /Game/MainLevel
```

### CLI surface

| Command | What it does |
|---------|--------------|
| `status` | Verify editor + plugin alive; report tool count + version |
| `tools list` / `describe` | Browse/inspect 160 MCP tools |
| `run NAME --args-json '{}'` | Generic dispatcher for any tool |
| `diagnostics` | Wraps `unreal.editor_diagnostics` |
| `automation list/run/report [--wait]` | Wraps `automation_*` with auto-poll |
| `pie-smoke [--map P]` | Wraps `pie_smoke` + auto-polls completion |
| `tasks list/describe/rate/pin` | Task Atlas wrappers |

Plus global flags: `--json` (machine output) / `--endpoint URL` / `--http-timeout SEC`

### Why this exists

UEAtelier previously was MCP-only. Agents like Claude Desktop and Codex Desktop speak MCP and could use it directly; everything else couldn't. This CLI gives every agent a path:
- Shell-script agents → subprocess + parse JSON
- CI bots → `cli-anything-ueatelier --json run unreal.compile_blueprint --args-json '{"path":"/Game/X"}'`
- Cursor command-mode → `cli-anything-ueatelier diagnostics`
- CLI-Anything Hub users → discoverable + installable via `cli-hub install ueatelier`

### Quality
- All validators PASS: registry 160, mirror 160, compat 0/0, verifier 0 blocking
- 18 pytest tests pass in 0.09s (mocked HTTP, no editor required)
- pip install + entry-point verified on Python 3.13
- Unreachable-endpoint JSON smoke clean (no Python traceback)
- 3-round Hermes prompt review caught 7 design ambiguities pre-dispatch (JSON-RPC method contract, output unwrapping, endpoint precedence, timeout disambiguation, status command exact behavior, invalid-args handling, count contradictions)

### Next
PM will open a registry-only PR to HKUDS/CLI-Anything adding UEAtelier to their CLI-Hub. Reference: `Tools/UEAtelierCli/SKILL.md` (399 lines, 10 sections matching their `cli-anything-blender` shape).

### Verify
```
sha256: <pending package_plugin.sh output>
```

#### Release Body

## Patch — Project Rebrand: UEvolve → UEAtelier

The project formerly known as **UEvolve** is now **UEAtelier**. No functional or technical changes — just branding to differentiate from the crowded `UnrealMCP*` GitHub space (28+ similar repos including [kvick-games/UnrealMCP](https://github.com/kvick-games/UnrealMCP) at 577★ and UnrealCopilot) and to drop the ambiguous "U-Evolve" pronunciation.

### Why "UEAtelier"
- **UE** is a 2-letter abbreviation with many meanings (lower trademark risk than the "Unreal" word, which is Epic Games' mark)
- **Atelier** (French for workshop) fits the self-extension workbench identity better than "evolve"
- Cleaner pronunciation: "U-E Atelier"

### What changed
- **Project branding**: README / AGENTS / docs all say "UEAtelier" now
- **Plugin Manager**: shows `UEAtelier` instead of `Unreal MCP`
- **Editor menus**: `Window > UEAtelier Chat`, `Window > UEAtelier Workbench`
- **Chat panel UI**: title + system message labels rebranded

### What did NOT change (intentional — preserves your existing install)
- Plugin folder `Plugins/UnrealMcp/` — directory name unchanged
- C++ module `UnrealMcp` — internal technical name unchanged
- Tool prefix `unreal.*` — MCP protocol identifiers stay
- HTTP endpoint `http://127.0.0.1:8765/mcp` — stays
- `Saved/UnrealMcp/` runtime directory — stays
- All `Tools/UnrealMcp*/` paths — stay
- Tool registry / categories — stay

Your existing project install will continue to work. Just the branding labels you see in the editor change. Internal references to "Unreal MCP plugin" in tool descriptions stay (technical accuracy).

### Quality
- Both engines build clean: UE 5.6 (UEvolveEditor) + UE 5.7 (MyProjectEditor)
- 64 files changed, 560 insertions / 560 deletions (1:1 rebrand replacements; no logic changes)
- Used `UEvolve(?![A-Za-z0-9_.])` regex to ONLY change product-name references in prose, NEVER renaming identifier suffixes (UEvolve.uproject filename, UEvolveEditor target, UEvolveExample dir, etc. all preserved)

### GitHub repo
The GitHub repo will be renamed `UEvolve` → `UEAtelier` shortly after this release. GitHub redirects keep old URLs working transparently.

### Verify
```
sha256: 736689d04ce1efd9084ae7e39cf09f335e81eab036143bd184742922f4ee4429
```

#### Release Body

## Patch — UE 5.6 Windows build fix

v0.22.0's `UnrealMcpAutomationTools.cpp:197` declared a local `FString LogPath` variable that shadowed UE's global `LogPath` log category declared in `EngineLogs.h`. Mac clang only warns (`-Wshadow`); Windows MSVC promotes C4459 to **error** under UE's default warning flags. Result: v0.22.0 source-only Windows zip extracted into a clean UE 5.6 project failed to compile.

Reported by Edwin's v0.22.0 Windows packaging validation 2026-05-19 with a patch attached.

### Fix
Single one-line variable rename in `UnrealMcpAutomationTools.cpp`:
- `LogPath` → `ProjectLogPath`

Pure local rename. No behavior change. No public API / schema / registry / package-layout change.

### Verified
- ✓ Mac UE 5.7 build clean
- ✓ Edwin's v0.22.0 Win-side validation (with this fix applied locally): clean UE 5.6 UBT compile + MCP headless smoke + `tools/list` count 150 (visible subset of 160 total)
- ✓ All validators PASS: registry 160, mirror 160, compat 0/0, verifier PASS

### Tooling improvements bundled
- **GitHub Actions Windows release packaging workflow** (`.github/workflows/win-release-package.yml`): auto-builds and attaches the Windows source-only zip on every tag push. No more manual Edwin-on-Windows step required for new releases.
- **`verify_package_integrity.py` scaffold fallback**: when checking the live repo, accepts `UnrealMcpToolScaffoldStarters/<id>/...` as a fallback for the gitignored `UnrealMcpToolScaffolds/<id>/...` working-copy path. Matches the v0.19.1 packager scripts' existing fallback.

### Verify
```
sha256: 98096a16f4f42fa1bbc141b469cfd8b95645f9eee9a664272b66fa3d7af43283
```
Extract the zip into your `<UserProject>/` root. **Windows users on v0.22.0 should upgrade** to avoid the C4459 build error.

#### Release Body

## What's New

`unreal.pie_smoke` — a single new MCP tool that verifies PIE (Play In Editor) can boot cleanly on a target map, stay alive briefly, and shut down to a sane editor state. Extends the existing `verification` category.

Registry: **159 → 160**, 11 categories.

### Why this exists

C1b was deferred at v0.20 until C1a (automation_*) accumulated real run data. With v0.20 + v0.21 shipped and the verification category mature, PIE smoke verification is now in scope. Provides AI clients with a first-class way to answer "does PIE actually boot on this project in this editor session?"

### Tool

```
unreal.pie_smoke({
  mapPath?: string,             // /Game/... World asset; validated before BeginPIE
  timeoutSeconds?: int = 60,    // clamp [10, 300]
  aliveWindowSeconds?: int = 5  // clamp [1, 30], must be < timeoutSeconds
})
```

Returns immediately with a runId; polled via the existing `automation_report` (shared state file namespace, shared single-active-run lock with v0.20 automation_*).

### Shared state & non-breaking automation_report extension

- State file in the SAME `Saved/UnrealMcp/AutomationRuns/<runId>.json` namespace
- Same `automation_report` polling tool — no new poll tool
- Non-breaking schema extension: new optional `runType: "automation" | "pie_smoke"` and `pieReport?: {...}` fields. Old v0.20 state files default to `"automation"` — full backward compatibility.

### `pieReport` shape

- `beganPlayObserved` / `aliveWindowSatisfied` / `pieEndedCleanly` — phase flags
- `diagnostics` — `errorCount` / `warningCount` + chronological-oldest excerpt (capped at 100) from v0.21 editor_diagnostics since PIE start. Full data still available via `unreal.editor_diagnostics({since: <startedAt>})`.
- `packageDirtinessDelta` — 4 path arrays: `dirtyAtStart` / `dirtyAtEnd` / `newlyDirty` / `cleanedDuringPie`
- `recoverabilityNote` — constant string reminder: PIE crash is NOT recoverable in-process; use `unreal_mcp_supervisor.py` to restart and re-run

### Lifecycle (18-step)

Server-side: validate args → validate mapPath → acquire shared active-run lock → capture diagnostics window start AND dirtyAtStart snapshot → optionally open map (rejects with `EditorMapDirty` if current map dirty and differs — no auto-save/discard) → register BeginPIE/EndPIE delegate handles → RequestPlaySession → wait for BeginPIE → alive window poll → RequestEndPlayMap → wait for EndPIE → unregister handles → dirtyAtEnd snapshot + diff → pull diagnostics → write final state → release lock.

Stale recovery same as v0.20: `startedAt + timeoutSeconds + 60s`.

### 5 structured error kinds

`RunAlreadyActive` (with `activeRunType` for cross-rejection between automation_* and pie_smoke), `EditorMapDirty`, `MapNotFound`, `InvalidMapPath`, `InvalidArguments`.

### Cross-rejection with automation_*

`automation_run` rejects when `pie_smoke` is active and vice versa. Same `errorKind: "RunAlreadyActive"`, `activeRunType` field disambiguates without introducing a new kind.

### Thread safety

All PIE API calls (`RequestPlaySession`, `RequestEndPlayMap`, delegate registration, `PlayWorld` access) marshalled to game thread via `AsyncTask(GameThread, ...)`. The FTSTicker that drives state transitions never calls PIE APIs from worker threads.

### What's NOT in v0.22

- Multi-PIE (dedicated server + client pairs) — separate chunk
- `pie_cancel` MCP tool — stop is best-effort via `RequestEndPlayMap`, no public cancel
- "Run automation test inside PIE" — that's C1c/C1d-sized future scope

### Quality
- All validators PASS: registry 160, mirror 160, compat 0/0, verifier 0 blocking
- ASCII-safety scan over 8 touched C++ files (including untracked new files) clean
- UE 5.6 (`UEvolveEditor`) and UE 5.7 (`MyProjectEditor`) both build clean
- Hermes coordinator flagged 5 PM-review concerns; runtime concerns analyzed and documented (deadlock risk is theoretical because UE's RequestPlaySession is deferred — added inline lock-ordering safety comment)

### Verify
```
sha256: e1ffdf5db1b330c4cc94b609eb65daf938b514b4aa1c731695fe9439bf120c9a
```
Extract the zip into your `<UserProject>/` root.

#### Release Body

## What's New

`unreal.editor_diagnostics` — a single new MCP tool in the `verification` category that lets AI clients distinguish real build errors from content warnings by querying a listener-backed Output Log ring buffer.

Registry: **158 → 159**, still 11 categories.

### Why this exists

Previously the AI client had no programmatic way to see what UE was actually logging — every error/warning looked the same from the outside. Common confusion: "Plugin failed to build" vs "stock Mannequin asset has a stale CustomVersion stamp" (the latter happens on every editor load but is harmless). `editor_diagnostics` returns structured entries with severity + domain class, plus optional one-line `suggested` hints for well-known patterns.

### Tool

```
unreal.editor_diagnostics({
  since?: "ISO-8601 UTC",
  classes?: ["compile"|"map_check"|"content"|"automation"|"log_warning"|"log_error"],
  limit?: 200    // max 1000
})
```

Returns entries chronological oldest → newest, each:
```
{ ts, severity, class, source, message, suggested? }
```

Plus envelope: `totalCount` / `truncated` / `ringBufferStartedAt` / `ringBufferOverflow` / `filteredClasses`.

### Architecture
- **5000-entry in-memory ring buffer** registered at module load via `GLog->AddOutputDevice` (no JSONL persistence)
- **Critical-section writes + snapshot-copy reads** — listener hot path adds no measurable overhead
- **Classification at write time** via pre-computed `LogCategory → DiagnosticClass` map (LogMapCheck/LogBlueprintEditor/LogKismet/LogLinker/LogAutomation/...). Unknown categories fall back to severity-based class. No regex in hot path.
- **`suggested` hint matching at read time** for 5 hardcoded high-confidence patterns:
  - `Package Version: 0` / `Min Required Version:` → resave asset
  - `_ExternalActors_` + `was not available` → save the parent umap
  - `Failed to load package` → check deletion / rename / EngineAssociation
  - `is not backwards compatible` → open with matching engine + resave
  - `Live Coding` → close editor or disable Live Coding before UBT

### Quality
- All validators PASS: registry 159, mirror 159, compat 0/0, verifier 0 blocking
- ASCII-safety scan over 7 touched C++ files (including untracked new files — Hermes flagged this in its self-audit)
- UE 5.6 (`UEvolveEditor`) and UE 5.7 (`MyProjectEditor`) both build clean

### Roadmap
Next: **v0.22 — C1b PIE Runtime Verification**. Hermes initially deferred C1b until C1a accumulated real run data; C1a (v0.20) shipped, so C1b is now in scope. Expect 2-3 strategic discussion rounds before drafting since PIE lifecycle is high-risk.

Extract the zip into your `<UserProject>/` root.

#### Release Body

## What's New

Closes the original v0.18 roadmap entry (C1a Verification Foundation) that got displaced by the Task Atlas program (v0.17 → v0.19), plus a UX polish on AI provider configuration. Registry grows from 155 → 158 in a new 11th category `verification`.

### v0.20 B1 — C1a Automation Tool Trio (registry 155 → 158)

Three new MCP tools in the new `verification` category wrap UE's Automation Test framework with an async polling pattern.

- `unreal.automation_list` — discover automation tests, filter+limit, read-only
- `unreal.automation_run` — start a named test, returns `runId` immediately (no game-thread blocking), single active run at a time, stale recovery if previous run wedged
- `unreal.automation_report` — poll runId for status/results/log excerpts

State file: `Saved/UnrealMcp/AutomationRuns/<runId>.json`. The handler returns before latent automation commands complete; ticking is driven by `FTSTicker` so the game thread is never starved.

### v0.20 B2 — Task Atlas Dogfood Gates + Watchdog Hardening

Three release-gate acceptance checks plus watchdog hardening on the automation runner.

**Gates:**
- **Gate A (manual)** — `task_label_backfill` LLM label quality checklist (≥4/5 reasonable)
- **Gate B (automated)** — `UnrealMcp.Verification.GateB.SkillReplay` C++ Automation Test exercises a read-only triad (`engine_version` → `project_settings_get` → `list_assets`) through Task Atlas's `[→ Skills]` → `skill_apply` chain
- **Gate D (automated)** — `UnrealMcp.Verification.GateD.RagHit` writes a synthetic Task Atlas markdown with a sentinel, refreshes the RAG index, queries `tool_recommend`, asserts the hit (RAII cleanup on assertion failure)
- **Gate C (deferred)** — Make Tool full apply chain is stretch / v0.20.1 hardening

**Watchdog hardening (internal-only state fields; public schema unchanged):**
- `lastHeartbeatUtc` refreshed every ticker invocation, persisted at most once per second (debounced)
- Two-window stale detection: `hard_timeout` (`startedAt + timeoutSeconds + 60s`) AND `unresponsive` (`now > lastHeartbeatUtc + 30s`)
- `bestEffortCancelAttempted` flag with `FAutomationTestFramework::DequeueAllCommands()` courtesy cleanup
- Module shutdown hook writes final `stale` state with reason `editor_shutdown`

### AI Settings Auto-Fill

In `Project Settings → Plugins → Unreal MCP → AI → Providers`, changing the **Kind** dropdown now auto-populates the canonical `BaseUrl` / `Model` / `CodexBinaryPath` defaults — only for fields that are currently empty (never overwrites your input). One-dropdown onboarding for common providers.

| Kind | Auto-filled defaults |
|------|---------------------|
| OpenAiResponses | `https://api.openai.com/v1/responses` + `gpt-5.1` |
| OpenAiChatCompat | placeholder hint (multi-vendor: Kimi/GLM/DeepSeek/Qwen/Ollama) |
| AnthropicMessages | `https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages` + `claude-sonnet-4-6` |
| Codex | `~/codex-orchestrator/bin/codex-agent` + `-m gpt-5.5 -r xhigh` |
| CodexAppServer | `http://127.0.0.1:8766` |

`ApiKey` is never auto-filled (user secret).

### Quality
- All validators PASS at every step: registry 158, mirror 158, compat 0/0, verifier 0 blocking
- ASCII-safety scan clean on all touched C++
- UE 5.6 (`UEvolveEditor` against `UEvolve.uproject`) and UE 5.7 (`MyProjectEditor` against `UEvolveExample57.uproject`) both build cleanly from same source
- Hermes coordinator caught a critical inverted-API-semantics bug in B1's automation ticker (`ExecuteLatentCommands` returns "done"; `ExecuteNetworkCommands` returns "has more") that would have stalled every non-Functional test in the runner — fixed pre-commit

### Strategic
This release closes the original v0.18 C1a roadmap entry (displaced by the Task Atlas v0.17 → v0.19 program). Tasks Atlas now has objective replay/RAG validation, and `automation_*` provides the foundation for future C1b (PIE runtime verification) which remains deferred until C1a accumulates real run data.

![UEvolve — Unreal MCP Self-Extension Workbench](https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEvolve/releases/download/v0.19.1/uevolve-task-atlas-overview.png)

> Cumulative release notes covering everything since v0.16.0: Task Atlas v0.17 → v0.18 → v0.19 program (3 versions, 8 commits) plus the v0.19.1 UE 5.6 build fix. Available in **English**, **中文**, and **日本語** below.

---

## English

### Overview

v0.19.1 closes a three-version program that adds **Task Atlas** — a chat-panel-driven workflow visualization layer that records, rates, pins, and promotes AI-driven tool workflows. Registry grew from 149 to 155 tools across one new `task-atlas` category. The 0.19.1 patch fixes a UE 5.6 build regression introduced by latent unity-build symbol collisions.

### What's in this release (cumulative since v0.16.0)

#### Task Atlas — v0.17.0 Foundation
- **5 new MCP tools** in the new `task-atlas` category (registry 149 → 154):
  - `unreal.activity_log_annotate` — chat panel writes user intent / AI summary events
  - `unreal.task_list` — query tasks by filter (`all` / `success` / `failed` / `unrated` / `pinned`)
  - `unreal.task_describe` — full task detail including critical path
  - `unreal.task_rate` — mark success / failed / unrated (user-mutable any time)
  - `unreal.task_pin` — pin or unpin a workflow
- **4 new ActivityLog `eventKind` values**: `user_intent`, `ai_summary`, `task_rating`, `task_pin_change`
- **Task persistence** at `Saved/UnrealMcp/Tasks/<taskId>.json` with a frozen v1 schema
- **Heuristic clustering**: same `sessionId` + 10-minute event gap (chosen from real ActivityLog distribution; ~99.7% of in-session gaps observed ≤ 10 min)
- **Chat panel** gets a Task Atlas toolbar button and inline 👍/👎 rating buttons under AI completion messages
- **New Slate window `STaskAtlasWindow`**: workflow rows with tool-sequence visualizers, an unused-tools section, a live search bar, and a tool detail popover
- **[Pin] button functional**; `[→ Skills]` / `[→ RAG]` / `[Make Tool]` visible but disabled with v0.18/v0.19 placeholders

#### Task Atlas — v0.18.0 Skills + RAG promote handlers
- **`[→ Skills]` activated**: invokes `unreal.skill_distill_from_activity` with the task's session and time window; produces a draft skill ready to review and promote
- **`[→ RAG]` activated**: writes `Saved/UnrealMcp/KnowledgeSources/TaskAtlas/<taskId>.md` with task label, rating, pinned flag, session, time range, user intent, AI summary, critical path, and compact event refs. Absolute home paths (`/Users/<name>/`) are redacted to `<HOME>/` for portability. Then triggers `unreal.knowledge_index_refresh`.

#### Task Atlas — v0.19.0 Make Tool + RAG indexing + LLM backfill
- **`[Make Tool]` activated**: derives a `toolId` from the task label (`atlas_<snake_case>`), builds `scaffold_mcp_tool` args from critical path and metadata, generates a scaffold the user can edit and apply via `unreal.mcp_extension_pipeline`
- **RAG indexing closure**: `unreal.knowledge_index_refresh` now scans `*.md` under `Saved/UnrealMcp/KnowledgeSources/TaskAtlas/`. Each markdown becomes an inline `task-atlas` KnowledgeCard, so promoted tasks are searchable after refresh — closes v0.18's deferred indexing gap
- **New tool `unreal.task_label_backfill`** (registry 154 → 155): opt-in batch tool that uses Anthropic `claude-haiku-4-5` (fallback `claude-sonnet-4-6`) to infer 3-7 word task labels for historical sessions lacking `user_intent`. Conservative skip heuristics — never overwrites pinned tasks or user-edited labels. Graceful degradation when no API key is configured.

#### v0.19.1 Patch — UE 5.6 build fix
- **Root cause**: `UnrealMcpEditorTools.cpp` carried a duplicate `IsEditorPlaying` / `MakePieBlockedResult` definition inside an anonymous namespace, while `UnrealMcpCoreHelpers.cpp` defines them at namespace scope. Several files also defined same-named per-file helpers in anonymous namespaces that collide under UBT unity build. UE 5.7 example-host builds were masked by adaptive unity exclusion; UE 5.6 dev-host builds against `UEvolve.uproject` exposed the issue.
- **Fix**: removed duplicate definitions, set `bUseUnity = false` for the UnrealMcp module. Per-file compilation eliminates the entire class of collision risk. Modest full-build slowdown, incremental builds unaffected.
- **Verified**: UE 5.6 `UEvolveEditor` and UE 5.7 `MyProjectEditor` both build clean from the same source.

### Quality
- All validators PASS at every step: registry (155), mirror (155), compat (0 errors / 0 warnings), package integrity (0 blocking / 0 warnings)
- ASCII-safety scan PASS on all touched C++ files
- 10/10 PASS on programmatic smoke for the 5 Task Atlas tools (filter semantics, rating mutability, type rejection)
- C++ Automation Tests + 7 JSON test fixtures under `Tools/UnrealMcpTests/TaskAtlas/`

### Verify
```

Win sha256: 098837dbd254be7497a479630326338c2908ed9c81e2672d8e3230f8332572d7
```
Extract the zip into your `<UserProject>/` root (next to the `.uproject`), **not** under `Plugins/`.

## 中文

### 概览

v0.19.1 收官一个跨越三个版本的程序——**Task Atlas**，一个由 chat 面板驱动的工作流可视化层，可以记录、评分、固定和推广 AI 驱动的工具工作流。Registry 从 149 个工具增长到 155 个，新增了一个 `task-atlas` 分类。0.19.1 修复了 UE 5.6 构建因潜在 unity-build 符号冲突导致的 regression。

### 本次发布内容（从 v0.16.0 之后累计）

#### Task Atlas — v0.17.0 基础层
- **5 个新 MCP 工具**，归入新增的 `task-atlas` 分类（registry 149 → 154）：
  - `unreal.activity_log_annotate` — chat 面板写入用户意图 / AI 总结事件
  - `unreal.task_list` — 按 filter 查询任务（`all` / `success` / `failed` / `unrated` / `pinned`）
  - `unreal.task_describe` — 返回单个任务的完整明细，含 critical path
  - `unreal.task_rate` — 评分 success / failed / unrated（用户可随时更改）
  - `unreal.task_pin` — 固定或取消固定一个工作流
- **4 个新的 ActivityLog `eventKind`**：`user_intent`、`ai_summary`、`task_rating`、`task_pin_change`
- **Task 持久化** 到 `Saved/UnrealMcp/Tasks/<taskId>.json`，使用冻结的 v1 schema
- **启发式聚类**：同一 `sessionId` + 10 分钟事件间隔（根据实际 ActivityLog 分布选定，约 99.7% 的会话内事件间隔 ≤ 10 分钟）
- **Chat 面板** 新增 Task Atlas 工具栏按钮 + AI 完成消息下方的 inline 👍/👎 评分按钮
- **新 Slate 窗口 `STaskAtlasWindow`**：工作流行带工具序列可视化、未使用工具区、实时搜索栏、工具详情 popover
- **`[Pin]` 按钮已实装**；`[→ Skills]` / `[→ RAG]` / `[Make Tool]` 可见但 disabled，标注 v0.18/v0.19 占位

#### Task Atlas — v0.18.0 Skills + RAG 推广出口
- **`[→ Skills]` 已激活**：调用 `unreal.skill_distill_from_activity`，传入任务的 sessionId 和时间窗口；生成 draft skill，等待审阅后推广
- **`[→ RAG]` 已激活**：写入 `Saved/UnrealMcp/KnowledgeSources/TaskAtlas/<taskId>.md`，包含任务 label、rating、pinned 标志、sessionId、时间范围、用户意图、AI 总结、critical path、紧凑 event refs。绝对家目录路径（`/Users/<name>/`）会被替换为 `<HOME>/` 以增加可移植性。之后触发 `unreal.knowledge_index_refresh`。

#### Task Atlas — v0.19.0 Make Tool + RAG 索引 + LLM 回溯标注
- **`[Make Tool]` 已激活**：从 task label 派生 `toolId`（`atlas_<snake_case>`），用 critical path + metadata 构造 `scaffold_mcp_tool` 参数，生成 scaffold；用户编辑后可用 `unreal.mcp_extension_pipeline` apply
- **RAG 索引闭环**：`unreal.knowledge_index_refresh` 现在会扫描 `Saved/UnrealMcp/KnowledgeSources/TaskAtlas/` 下的 `*.md`。每个 markdown 成为内联的 `task-atlas` KnowledgeCard，因此推广过的任务在 refresh 后可被搜索——补上 v0.18 推迟的索引缺口
- **新工具 `unreal.task_label_backfill`**（registry 154 → 155）：opt-in 批处理工具，使用 Anthropic `claude-haiku-4-5`（fallback `claude-sonnet-4-6`）为缺少 `user_intent` 的历史 session 推断 3-7 词任务 label。保守的 skip 启发式——绝不覆盖固定任务或用户编辑过的 label。无 API key 时优雅降级。

#### v0.19.1 补丁 — UE 5.6 构建修复
- **根因**：`UnrealMcpEditorTools.cpp` 在匿名 namespace 里带了一份 `IsEditorPlaying` / `MakePieBlockedResult` 的重复定义，而 `UnrealMcpCoreHelpers.cpp` 在 namespace scope 也定义了同名函数。多个文件还在匿名 namespace 中定义了同名的 per-file helper，在 UBT unity build 下合并到同一 TU 时冲突。UE 5.7 example host 构建被 adaptive unity 排除巧合掩盖了；UE 5.6 dev host 构建（`UEvolve.uproject`）暴露了问题。
- **修复**：删除了重复定义，并为 UnrealMcp 模块设置 `bUseUnity = false`。逐文件编译消除了整类冲突风险。完整构建略慢，增量构建不变。
- **验证**：UE 5.6 `UEvolveEditor` 和 UE 5.7 `MyProjectEditor` 用同一份 source 都构建通过。

### 质量
- 每一步的所有 validator 都 PASS：registry（155）、mirror（155）、compat（0 errors / 0 warnings）、package integrity（0 blocking / 0 warnings）
- 所有改动的 C++ 文件 ASCII-safety 扫描 PASS
- 5 个 Task Atlas 工具的 programmatic smoke 10/10 PASS（filter 语义、rating 可变更性、类型拒绝）
- C++ Automation Tests + 7 个 JSON 测试 fixture 位于 `Tools/UnrealMcpTests/TaskAtlas/`

## 日本語

### 概要

v0.19.1 は **Task Atlas** という 3 バージョンにわたるプログラムを完成させます。Task Atlas は chat パネル駆動のワークフロー可視化レイヤーで、AI ツールワークフローを記録・評価・固定・昇格できます。Registry は 149 ツールから 155 ツールに増え、新カテゴリ `task-atlas` が 1 つ追加されました。v0.19.1 パッチは UE 5.6 ビルドで発生していた unity-build シンボル衝突起因の regression を修正します。

### このリリースの内容（v0.16.0 以降の累積）

#### Task Atlas — v0.17.0 基盤
- 新カテゴリ `task-atlas` に **5 つの新規 MCP ツール**（registry 149 → 154）：
  - `unreal.activity_log_annotate` — chat パネルから user intent / AI summary イベントを書き込み
  - `unreal.task_list` — filter で task を照会（`all` / `success` / `failed` / `unrated` / `pinned`）
  - `unreal.task_describe` — 1 件の task の詳細（critical path を含む）
  - `unreal.task_rate` — success / failed / unrated を設定（ユーザーがいつでも変更可能）
  - `unreal.task_pin` — ワークフローを固定 / 解除
- **4 つの新 ActivityLog `eventKind`**：`user_intent`、`ai_summary`、`task_rating`、`task_pin_change`
- **Task 永続化**：`Saved/UnrealMcp/Tasks/<taskId>.json`、凍結された v1 スキーマ
- **ヒューリスティッククラスタリング**：同一 `sessionId` ＋ 10 分のイベント間隔（実際の ActivityLog 分布から決定。約 99.7% のセッション内ギャップが 10 分以下）
- **Chat パネル**に Task Atlas ツールバーボタンと、AI 完了メッセージの下にインライン 👍/👎 評価ボタンを追加
- **新 Slate ウィンドウ `STaskAtlasWindow`**：ワークフロー行（ツール列ビジュアライザ付き）、未使用ツールセクション、ライブ検索バー、ツール詳細ポップオーバー
- **`[Pin]` ボタンは機能**；`[→ Skills]` / `[→ RAG]` / `[Make Tool]` は表示されるが無効化、v0.18/v0.19 のプレースホルダーを表示

#### Task Atlas — v0.18.0 Skills + RAG 昇格ハンドラ
- **`[→ Skills]` 有効化**：task の sessionId と時間範囲を渡して `unreal.skill_distill_from_activity` を呼び出し、レビュー＆昇格可能な draft skill を生成
- **`[→ RAG]` 有効化**：`Saved/UnrealMcp/KnowledgeSources/TaskAtlas/<taskId>.md` に task label、rating、pinned フラグ、sessionId、時間範囲、user intent、AI summary、critical path、コンパクトな event refs を書き出し。ホーム絶対パス（`/Users/<name>/`）はポータビリティのため `<HOME>/` に変換。そのあと `unreal.knowledge_index_refresh` を呼び出し。

#### Task Atlas — v0.19.0 Make Tool + RAG インデックス + LLM バックフィル
- **`[Make Tool]` 有効化**：task label から `toolId`（`atlas_<snake_case>`）を導出し、critical path とメタデータから `scaffold_mcp_tool` の引数を組み立て、scaffold を生成。ユーザーは編集後 `unreal.mcp_extension_pipeline` で apply できます
- **RAG インデックスのクローズアウト**：`unreal.knowledge_index_refresh` が `Saved/UnrealMcp/KnowledgeSources/TaskAtlas/` 配下の `*.md` をスキャンするように。各 markdown はインラインの `task-atlas` KnowledgeCard になり、昇格済み task は refresh 後に検索可能に——v0.18 で延期されていたインデックスのギャップを解消
- **新ツール `unreal.task_label_backfill`**（registry 154 → 155）：オプトインのバッチツールで、Anthropic `claude-haiku-4-5`（フォールバック `claude-sonnet-4-6`）を使い、`user_intent` がない過去 session に 3-7 単語の task label を推論。保守的なスキップヒューリスティック——固定済み task やユーザー編集済み label は決して上書きしません。API キー未設定時は graceful degradation。

#### v0.19.1 パッチ — UE 5.6 ビルド修正
- **根本原因**：`UnrealMcpEditorTools.cpp` が匿名 namespace の中に `IsEditorPlaying` / `MakePieBlockedResult` の重複定義を持ち、`UnrealMcpCoreHelpers.cpp` は namespace スコープで同名関数を定義していました。さらに複数ファイルが匿名 namespace 内に同名の per-file helper を定義していて、UBT unity build で 1 TU にまとめられた時に衝突。UE 5.7 example host ビルドは adaptive unity exclusion で偶然マスクされていましたが、UE 5.6 dev host（`UEvolve.uproject`）でこの問題が顕在化しました。
- **修正**：重複定義を削除し、UnrealMcp モジュールに `bUseUnity = false` を設定。ファイルごとのコンパイルでこの種の衝突リスクを根本から排除。フルビルドは少し遅くなりますが、増分ビルドは影響なし。
- **検証**：UE 5.6 `UEvolveEditor` と UE 5.7 `MyProjectEditor` の両方が、同じソースから clean に build 成功。

### 品質
- 各ステップで全 validator PASS：registry（155）、mirror（155）、compat（0 errors / 0 warnings）、package integrity（0 blocking / 0 warnings）
- 触れた C++ ファイル全てに対する ASCII-safety スキャン PASS
- Task Atlas の 5 ツールについてのプログラマティック smoke は 10/10 PASS（filter セマンティクス、rating 可変性、型拒否）
- C++ Automation Tests と 7 つの JSON テスト fixture が `Tools/UnrealMcpTests/TaskAtlas/` にあります
