#### Release Body

## What's New

**Completes the Task Atlas 3-version program** (v0.17 → v0.18 → v0.19). All 4 promote buttons in the Task Atlas window are now functional, RAG indexing covers task-promoted markdown, and historical sessions without `user_intent` can be auto-labeled via LLM.

### Three deliverables landed

**A. [Make Tool] button activated** (commit f186c96)
- Derives a `toolId` from task label (atlas_<snake_case>)
- Builds args for `unreal.scaffold_mcp_tool` from the task's critical path and metadata
- Generates a scaffold the user can edit and apply via `unreal.mcp_extension_pipeline`

**B. RAG indexing for Task Atlas markdown** (commit ada09ba)
- Extends `unreal.knowledge_index_refresh` to scan `*.md` under `Saved/UnrealMcp/KnowledgeSources/TaskAtlas/`
- Each markdown becomes an inline `task-atlas` KnowledgeCard
- Closes v0.18's deferred indexing gap — promoted tasks are now searchable

**C. `unreal.task_label_backfill`** (commit fab1b21) — new tool (155 total)
- Opt-in batch tool using Anthropic claude-haiku-4-5 (fallback claude-sonnet-4-6)
- Infers 3-7 word task labels for historical sessions lacking `user_intent`
- Conservative skip heuristics: never overwrites pinned tasks; only processes placeholder labels matching "Session YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"
- Graceful degradation when API key not configured
- Returns structured `{processedCount, updatedCount, skippedCount, skippedReasons, ...}`

### Registry
- 154 → **155** (one new tool: `unreal.task_label_backfill`)
- All 8 categories retained; `task-atlas` now has 6 tools total

### Task Atlas program summary

| Version | Theme | Key delivery |
|---------|-------|--------------|
| v0.17.0 | Foundation | Data layer + 5 tools + UI shell + Pin |
| v0.18.0 | Light promotes | [→ Skills] + [→ RAG] (RAG indexing deferred) |
| **v0.19.0** | **Heavy promote + closure** | **[Make Tool] + RAG indexing + LLM backfill** |

Total Task Atlas program: ~80 files touched, ~5300 LOC added across 3 versions, 1 new MCP category, 6 new MCP tools, 1 new Slate window, chat panel toolbar button + inline rating affordances.

- UE 5.7 Mac build verified for each part

#### Release Body

## What's New

Activates the [→ Skills] and [→ RAG] buttons in Task Atlas that were v0.17 placeholders. No new tools or schema changes — only fills handler implementations as the v0.17 architecture intended.

### [→ Skills] — fully functional
- Invokes `unreal.skill_distill_from_activity` with the task's `sessionId`, label-derived skill name, `title` from label, `goal` from `userIntentText`, `writeDraft=true`, `overwrite=true`
- Status surfaces the produced draft skill path
- Use case: turn a task workflow into a parameterizable, reusable skill in `Tools/UnrealMcpSkills/`

### [→ RAG] — writes source, indexing deferred to v0.19
- Writes `Saved/UnrealMcp/KnowledgeSources/TaskAtlas/<taskId>.md` with: task label, rating, pinned flag, sessionId, time range, user intent, AI summary, critical path, compact event refs
- Sanitizes absolute home paths (`/Users/<name>/` → `<HOME>/`) for portability
- Calls `unreal.knowledge_index_refresh` after the write
- **Known limitation**: `knowledge_index_refresh` currently scans `documents.jsonl` manifest files, not arbitrary `*.md` under the source root. The Task Atlas markdown is written reliably but is not yet picked up by the RAG index. The indexing extension lands in v0.19 alongside the Make Tool integration.

### [Make Tool] — still v0.19 placeholder

### Quality
- All validators PASS: registry 154 (unchanged), mirror 154, compat 0/0, verifier PASS
- UE 5.7 Mac build verified
- ASCII-safety scan PASS
- 6 files changed, +426/-17 LOC

```

#### Release Body

## What's New

**Task Atlas** — a chat-panel-driven workflow visualization system that records AI-driven workflows, lets users rate them success/fail, and pin successful ones against future re-clustering. This is the **foundation** release; promote-to-skill / promote-to-RAG land in v0.18, and promote-to-tool + LLM retrospective labeling in v0.19.

### What v0.17 ships

**Data layer**
- 4 new ActivityLog eventKinds: `user_intent`, `ai_summary`, `task_rating`, `task_pin_change`
- Task persistence under `Saved/UnrealMcp/Tasks/<taskId>.json` with v1 schema
- Heuristic clustering: same `sessionId` + 10-min event gap (chosen from real ActivityLog distribution)
- Pinned tasks freeze critical path against future re-clustering

**5 new MCP tools** (149 → 154) — new `task-atlas` category (10th)
- `unreal.activity_log_annotate` — chat panel writes user intent / AI summary
- `unreal.task_list` — query tasks (filter by all/success/failed/unrated/pinned)
- `unreal.task_describe` — full task detail including critical path
- `unreal.task_rate` — set rating (mutable any time)
- `unreal.task_pin` — pin / unpin

**UI shell** (chat-panel-only by design)
- "Task Atlas" toolbar button in ChatPanel opens new Slate window
- Inline 👍/👎 rating buttons under AI completion messages
- Workflows section with tool-sequence rows; unused tools below; live search bar at bottom; tool detail popover
- `[Pin]` button functional; `[Make Tool]` / `[→ Skills]` / `[→ RAG]` visible with "Coming in v0.18/v0.19" placeholders

### Quality
- Programmatic smoke: **10/10 PASS** (all 5 tools, type rejection, enum validation, filter semantics, rating mutability)
- ASCII-safety scan: PASS (5 non-ASCII glyphs replaced during dispatch review)
- All validators: PASS (registry 154, mirror 154, compat 0/0, verifier pass)
- C++ Automation Tests + 5 JSON fixtures under `Tools/UnrealMcpTests/TaskAtlas/`

### Cross-version invariants locked in v0.17

These are frozen — v0.18 and v0.19 will only fill promote handler implementations, never change them:
- Task JSON v1 schema
- 4 ActivityLog eventKinds
- 5 tool signatures
- UI 4-button layout

## What's New

**8 new MCP tools** (registry 141 → 149), closing the UMG editing asymmetry and adding the first Material Instance parameter surface.

### Widget Edit Tools (4)
- `unreal.widget_rename` — rename with binding/reference preservation (delegate, animation, navigation, Blueprint variable)
- `unreal.widget_reorder_child` — reorder siblings in a panel by index
- `unreal.widget_duplicate` — copy widget + optional subtree with unique name generation
- `unreal.widget_delete` — guarded delete; refuses when bindings exist unless `force=true`

### Material Instance Tools (4) — new `material` category
- `unreal.material_instance_list` — discover MI assets under a content path
- `unreal.material_instance_get_parameters` — read scalar/vector/texture/static switch params
- `unreal.material_instance_set_scalar` — type-strict float set with `TypeMismatch` rejection
- `unreal.material_instance_set_vector` — type-strict RGBA object set

### Quality
- All 8 tools pass editor smoke tests (material create+read+write, widget reorder+duplicate+rename+delete)
- Type rejection verified: string "0.5" → `errorKind: TypeMismatch`
- C++ Automation Tests cover binding preservation, delete refusal, duplicate collision, and strict value parsing
- 8 JSON test fixtures in `Tools/UnrealMcpTests/Widget/` and `Material/`

#### Release Body

**v0.15.2 — C5 complete: install verification UI surfacing + Fab submission readiness docs**

Patch release on top of [v0.15.1](https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEvolve/releases/tag/v0.15.1). Registry tool count unchanged at **141**. Marks the end of the C5 (Marketplace / Install UX hardening) initiative — all 4 deliverable groups from the brainstorm scope are now landed.

## What's new since v0.15.1

### Slate Workbench install doctor card ([commit d1fc4d8](https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEvolve/commit/d1fc4d8))

`Window > Unreal MCP Workbench` now renders an "Install Doctor" section between the existing stats grid and the Last Result border. The v0.15.1 `mcp_workbench_status` backend already published these fields (`installDoctorFound`, `installDoctorSummary`, `installDoctorLatestPath`); v0.15.2 exposes them visually.

| Element | Source |
|---|---|
| Status badge (color-coded) | `installDoctorSummary.overallSeverity` — pass/warning/error/pending |
| Last-run timestamp | `installDoctorSummary.lastRunUtc` |
| Validator version label | `installDoctorSummary.validatorVersion` (e.g. `0.15.0-c5-1b`) |
| Issue summary | `X blocking \| Y warnings \| Z passes` |
| Scrollable per-check rows | `installDoctorSummary.checks[]` — severity badge + id + summary |
| "Re-run install doctor" button | calls `unreal.install_doctor` with `refresh: true`, then auto-refetches `mcp_workbench_status` so the card updates from the new cached state |
| "Open latest.json folder" button | `FPlatformProcess::ExploreFolder` on the parent directory of `installDoctorLatestPath` |

Pending state: if the first-run auto-probe has not yet completed (or the user has not run the tool manually), the badge reads "Pending" in grey and the check list shows "(no checks yet)".

**ASCII-safe display strings only.** During Hermes coordinator review, Codex initially used em-dash (`—`) and middle-dot (`·`) Unicode characters in raw C++ string literals. Hermes flagged the Windows MSVC source-encoding risk and requested an ASCII fix before delivery; final commit uses `-` and `|` exclusively.

### Fab/Marketplace submission readiness checklist ([commit 41cdb84](https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEvolve/commit/41cdb84))

`Docs/FabSubmissionChecklist.md` (279 lines, 18 sections) is the canonical pre-submission walkthrough for publishing UEvolve on Fab (Epic's marketplace successor that replaced Unreal Engine Marketplace, Sketchfab, Quixel Bridge, and ArtStation Marketplace in late 2024).

The doc maps each Fab review item to the file or process in this repository that supplies the evidence. When PM is ready to actually submit, they walk it top-to-bottom and the doc says where each piece of evidence lives OR what gap to close.

Includes a 12-item numbered action list of submission-blocking gaps (icon, screenshots, seller name, support email, plugin-only repackage variant, Linux verification, UE 5.8 forward-compat probe, optional sizzle video, etc.).

## C5 milestone summary

With v0.15.2, the C5 (Marketplace / Install UX hardening) initiative is **functionally complete**. All 4 deliverable groups from the original brainstorm scope have landed:

| Group | Deliverable | Chunk |
|---|---|---|
| A | First-run editor doctor | 1b — `unreal.install_doctor` MCP tool (read-only, low risk) |
| B | Duplicate plugin detector | 1b subset — `duplicate_plugin_conflict` check (bounded 4-candidate scan + optional 2-level `deepScanEnginePlugins`) |
| C | Standalone packaging verifier | 1a — `Tools/verify_package_integrity.py` (13 invariant checks, cross-platform, `--root` / `--zip` / `--mode source` / `--mode full-win` modes) |
| D | Marketplace/Fab submission readiness | 2b — `Docs/FabSubmissionChecklist.md` |
| + | Slate UI surfacing | 2a — Workbench install doctor card |
| + | 100% registry metadata coverage | 1a-docs — 118 description fills + 127 title fills |

## Install

1. Download `UnrealMcp-v0.15.2-mac-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip`.
2. Extract into your existing project root (the directory containing your `.uproject`), **not** under `Plugins/`. The zip contains `Plugins/UnrealMcp/...` at its root, plus shared `Tools/...`, `Docs/...`, and `Schemas/...` assets.
3. Open the `.uproject`. The editor will offer to compile the new plugin source on first launch.
4. After launch: open `Window > Unreal MCP Workbench` and you'll see the new Install Doctor card directly. The first-run auto-probe writes `Saved/UnrealMcp/InstallDoctor/latest.json` during `OnPostEngineInit` (deferred via `AsyncTask(GameThread)` so editor cold-start is not blocked); the card reads it via the existing "Refresh status" flow.

See `Plugins/UnrealMcp/INSTALL.md` (or `Tools/PackagingResources/INSTALL.md` in the source tree) for full instructions.

## Windows zip

Will be uploaded to this same release once the Win full-experience build is regenerated against `v0.15.2`. Combining the previously-pending v0.15.1 Win build into this release means the Win-side user only needs to rebuild once. Track via issue comments. The Mac zip linked here is source-only; both Mac UE 5.6/5.7 and Win UE 5.6/5.7 are supported once UBT compiles the source against your engine.

## Compatibility

- UE 5.6.1 ✓ (Mac, Win)
- UE 5.7.4 ✓ (Mac, Win)
- Linux: not verified (declared in `Docs/FabSubmissionChecklist.md` § 12 as a known gap)
- UE 5.8: not yet probed (declared in checklist § 6 as a future action item)

#### Release Body

**v0.15.1 — install verification trinity**

Patch release bundling three sub-chunks that together harden the install / packaging / runtime self-check surface. Registry: **140 → 141 tools**.

## What's new

### 1. `Tools/verify_package_integrity.py` — standalone cross-platform package verifier ([commit 11b4682](https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEvolve/commit/11b4682))

13 invariant checks runnable against a live repo OR a built zip:
- registry mirror byte-equal
- schema canonical/mirror/alias byte-equal
- no git symlink stubs (Windows clone trap defense)
- required files present (mode-specific: `source`, `full-win`)
- excluded paths absent (`Saved/`, `Intermediate/`, `Binaries/`, `node_modules/`, etc.)
- Win64 binary present (full-win mode only)
- bridge runtime bundled (full-win mode only)
- INSTALL.md present
- FIRST_LAUNCH.md present
- registry + schema JSON valid
- sha256 sidecar matches zip (--zip mode only)
- schema alias not Win symlink stub

Flags: `--root <path> | --zip <path>`, `--mode source|full-win`, `--strict|--lenient`, `--json`. Vocabulary versioned as `validatorVersion: 0.15.0-c5-1a`. Docs: `Docs/PackagingIntegrity.md`.

### 2. 100% registry metadata coverage ([commit 5f4a8af](https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEvolve/commit/5f4a8af))

Every one of the 140 (now 141) registry tools now has both `title` (2-5 word Title Case verb+subject) and `description` (1-3 sentences, what + when + side-effect). Canonical and plugin-mirror JSON stay byte-equal; `UnrealMcpToolRegistrar.cpp` `MakeDescriptor` strings aligned with JSON. This unblocks Chat panel tool cards, Workbench tool-list rendering, and `tools/list` clarity for downstream AI clients.

Coverage: descriptions 22/140 → 140/140; titles 13/140 → 140/140.

### 3. `unreal.install_doctor` — read-only editor-runtime MCP tool ([commit 4eccdbc](https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEvolve/commit/4eccdbc))

New tool in the `self-extension` category (read-only, low risk). Reuses the 1a invariant vocabulary as `validatorVersion: 0.15.0-c5-1b` and layers **4 editor-runtime checks** on top of the Python verifier's static set:

| Check ID | What it does |
|---|---|
| `python_script_plugin_enabled` | `IPluginManager` state probe — without `PythonScriptPlugin` enabled, `pythonImportAllowList` enforcement and the `unreal.python_runtime_info` tool can't function. |
| `mcp_endpoint_listening` | TCP probe of `127.0.0.1:8765` with **100 ms** timeout — verifies the MCP streamable-HTTP server is reachable from a localhost client. |
| `bridge_port_reachable` | TCP probe of `127.0.0.1:8766` with **100 ms** timeout — verifies the Codex App Server bridge daemon is reachable (5-state `EInstallDoctorPortState`: listening / refused / unreachable / timeout / error). |
| `duplicate_plugin_conflict` | Bounded **4-candidate** scan of `<Project>/Plugins/UnrealMcp`, the mounted plugin `BaseDir`, `<Engine>/Plugins/UnrealMcp`, `<Engine>/Plugins/Marketplace/UnrealMcp` — flags the trap where engine-level and project-level installs silently shadow each other. Optional `deepScanEnginePlugins: true` adds a 2-level recursive walk. |

Writes structured envelope to `<Project>/Saved/UnrealMcp/InstallDoctor/latest.json` on each run and embeds the latest summary into `mcp_workbench_status` under `installDoctorFound` / `installDoctorSummary` / `installDoctorLatestPath`. The first-run probe defers via `AsyncTask(ENamedThreads::GameThread)` scheduled from `FUnrealMcpModule::StartupModule`, so editor cold-start time is unaffected.

`DetectDuplicateUnrealMcpPlugins` is exposed as a pure function for testability; the C++ Automation Test (`UnrealMcpInstallDoctorTests.cpp`) covers single-mounted / two-different-candidates (conflict) / trailing-slash + missing-descriptor de-duplication, and the JSON fixture (`Tools/UnrealMcpTests/SelfExtension/40_install_doctor_duplicate_conflict.json`) exercises the dispatcher path via hidden `_testDuplicatePluginCandidates` + `_testMountedPluginPath` injection without extending the public schema.

1. Download `UnrealMcp-v0.15.1-mac-ue56-ue57-projectroot.zip`.

#### Release Body

## UnrealMcp v0.14.0-python-track-mac — Self-extension closed-loop rework + Python tools + v0.15 chunk 1 (macOS)

This is the **macOS-only** cut of the v0.14.0-python-track milestone. It bundles
the self-extension closed-loop rework, the Python tool bridge, and the v0.15
chunk 1 C++ readback inspectors that landed on top of the original v0.14 tag.
Mac users (UE 5.6 / 5.7) can install from the projectroot zip below today; the
full-experience Windows zip is still pending verifier PASS and will publish
under the separate `v0.14.0-python-track` tag (currently a draft prerelease).

The self-extension loop can now safely cross from C++ registry tools into
Python-backed Unreal Editor automation. The apply pipeline is atomic,
disk-verified, dependency-aware, and able to plan required C++ includes and
Build.cs modules before mutation. Python-track tools are registered in the
normal manifest, shown by `tools/list`, dispatched through the MCP path, logged
in ActivityLog, hash-checked, path-restricted, and import-allow-list enforced.
This tag also exposes Blueprint graph mutation primitives to Python via
`UUnrealMcpBlueprintGraphLibrary` and closes the FPS bootstrap loop with fresh
end-to-end coverage.

### What's New

- **Atomic scaffold apply** with disk-verified rollback on partial failure
- **Rollback + status** now verify actual disk state vs manifest hashes
- **Brace-aware C++ scanner** replaces fragile anchor substring search
- **CategoryDispatcherBranch conflict checks** scoped to resolved dispatcher bodies
- **Registry implementationTrack metadata** with 4 new optional fields
- **Python tool bridge** + dispatcher interception + ActivityLog wiring
- **First Python-track tool**: `unreal.editor.python_runtime_info` (read-only smoke)
- **`tools/list` emits Python-track manifest entries** (previously C++-descriptor-only)
- **`pythonImportAllowList`** enforced via runtime `__import__` hook
- **`buildRequirements`** plans + applies includes and `.Build.cs` module dependencies
- **`dependsOn`** topological apply with DFS cycle / self / missing detection
- **`UUnrealMcpBlueprintGraphLibrary`** exposes 9 Blueprint graph mutation methods to Python (`add_call_function_node`, `add_input_axis_event_node`, `add_get_actor_forward_vector_node`, `add_get_actor_right_vector_node`, `connect_pins_by_guid`, `compile_blueprint`, `add_movement_input_call_node`, `add_controller_yaw_input_call_node`, `add_controller_pitch_input_call_node`)
- **FPS convenience wrappers** + closing 14/14 e2e test (BP creation → 4 InputAxis events → 5 call nodes → 4 wires → compile clean) on Mac UE 5.7.4

### v0.15 chunk 1 included — C++ readback inspectors

This zip also ships the v0.15 chunk 1 work that landed after the original
v0.14 tag. Three new read-only C++ tools close the Lane V get/inspect gap
called out in v0.14 "Known Limitations":

- **`unreal.actor_get_property`** — reads a UProperty value (dot-paths supported)
  off a named actor; structured errors for `ACTOR_NOT_FOUND` /
  `PROPERTY_NOT_FOUND` / `UNSUPPORTED_PROPERTY_TYPE`. Safe during PIE.
- **`unreal.actor_get_transform`** — reads world or relative transform with
  `location` / `rotation` / `scale` / `parentActorPath`; `INVALID_SPACE` for
  unknown space tokens.
- **`unreal.project_settings_get`** — reads project-settings keys across six
  categories (`input` / `rendering` / `game` / `engine` / `editor` /
  `physics`) via `UDeveloperSettings` reflection with a raw-ini config
  fallback.

Registry total moves from 120 to 123. Mirror match (`cmp -s`) preserved.

### Packager fixes baked in

Two projectroot zip fixes that surfaced during Mac Stage 2 e2e are included:

- Complete project-root overlay: zip now ships `Tools/UnrealMcpToolRegistry/`,
  `UnrealMcpSkills/`, `UnrealMcpKnowledge/`, `UnrealMcpTests/`,
  `UnrealMcpCodexBridge/` (source-only), and `Docs/FIRST_LAUNCH.md` alongside
  `Plugins/UnrealMcp/` and `Tools/UnrealMcpPyTools/`.
- Pre-staged scaffold working copies: zip now ships
  `Tools/UnrealMcpToolScaffolds/fps_bootstrap/` and
  `verify_input_drives_pawn/` so `mcp_apply_scaffold` resolves them without
  a manual scaffold-clone step.

### Known Limitations (still open in v0.15)

- **Migration tools** — no asset move / redirector fixup / dependency remap / project-version migration toolchain yet (v0.15 backlog)
- **Blueprint refactor** — no node delete / variable+function rename+delete / macro+interface editing (v0.15 chunk 2 in flight)
- **Recipe catalog** — only 3 named recipes (`first_person_ground_character`, `widget_hud`, `mcp_self_extension_pipeline`); v0.15 chunk 3 adds `rts_camera`, `top_down_input`, `hud_dashboard`, `asset_naming_audit`
- **UBT target matrix** — only `mcp_build_editor`; no `build_game` / `build_server` / `build_client` / `build_packaged` (v0.15 chunk 4)

### How to Install

See `Docs/FIRST_LAUNCH.md` inside the source tree for the trilingual quickstart. Source users also read `Plugins/UnrealMcp/INSTALL.md` inside the zip.

The Mac source-only zip is now a **project-root overlay**: extract it next to `<YourProject>.uproject` (NOT into `Plugins/`). You'll get:
- `<YourProject>/Plugins/UnrealMcp/` — full plugin source for UBT to build
- `<YourProject>/Tools/UnrealMcpPyTools/` — project-level Python tool handlers
- `<YourProject>/Tools/UnrealMcpToolScaffoldStarters/` — canonical scaffold templates for `mcp_apply_scaffold`

Then enable both `PythonScriptPlugin` and `UnrealMcp` in `<YourProject>.uproject`'s `Plugins` array and open the project. UBT compiles the plugin against your local UE 5.6 / 5.7 install on first launch (30s–15min depending on cache).

#### Release Body

## UnrealMcp v0.14.0-python-track — Windows full-experience (UE 5.6.1)

This is the **Windows full-experience cut** of the v0.14.0-python-track milestone, including prebuilt UE 5.6.1 Win64 plugin binaries baked into the zip. Drop-in: extract the projectroot zip next to `<YourProject>.uproject` (NOT under `Plugins/`), open the project, no UBT compile required because the Win64 plugin DLL ships in the zip.

Windows source-only cloners and macOS users should use the parallel [`v0.14.0-python-track-mac`](https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEvolve/releases/tag/v0.14.0-python-track-mac) release — that's source-only and lets UBT compile against your local UE install.

Beyond the original v0.14 milestone, this Windows release bundles the full v0.15 chunks 1-5 + Tier 1-5 Windows compatibility fixes (issue #2 saga: LogType C4459, Python allow-list + import-hook CPython kwarg compliance, fps_bootstrap dependsOn sync, AIAssistant optional, scaffold reader Starters fallback for fresh clones, Codex App Server bridge stdio + Win local Codex binary preference + bundled bun.exe launchers, six-class tool quality batch including project_settings_get effective runtime flag / bp_list_graph_nodes path normalize / tail_log multi-candidate fallback / save_dirty_packages skipReason / capture_project_snapshot actor capture metadata / 9-tool description sharpening) plus the cross-platform schema-symlink → real-file fix (commit 8917f99) that unblocked clean Windows clone packaging.

The self-extension loop can now safely cross from C++ registry tools into Python-backed Unreal Editor automation. The apply pipeline is atomic, disk-verified, dependency-aware, and able to plan required C++ includes and Build.cs modules before mutation. Python-track tools are registered in the normal manifest, shown by `tools/list`, dispatched through the MCP path, logged in ActivityLog, hash-checked, path-restricted, and import-allow-list enforced. This tag also exposes Blueprint graph mutation primitives to Python via `UUnrealMcpBlueprintGraphLibrary` and closes the FPS bootstrap loop with fresh end-to-end coverage.

### What's New

- **Atomic scaffold apply** with disk-verified rollback on partial failure
- **Rollback + status** now verify actual disk state vs manifest hashes
- **Brace-aware C++ scanner** replaces fragile anchor substring search
- **CategoryDispatcherBranch conflict checks** scoped to resolved dispatcher bodies
- **Registry implementationTrack metadata** with 4 new optional fields
- **Python tool bridge** + dispatcher interception + ActivityLog wiring
- **First Python-track tool**: `unreal.editor.python_runtime_info` (read-only smoke)
- **`tools/list` emits Python-track manifest entries** (previously C++-descriptor-only)
- **`pythonImportAllowList`** enforced via runtime `__import__` hook
- **`buildRequirements`** plans + applies includes and `.Build.cs` module dependencies
- **`dependsOn`** topological apply with DFS cycle / self / missing detection
- **`UUnrealMcpBlueprintGraphLibrary`** exposes 9 Blueprint graph mutation methods to Python (`add_call_function_node`, `add_input_axis_event_node`, `add_get_actor_forward_vector_node`, `add_get_actor_right_vector_node`, `connect_pins_by_guid`, `compile_blueprint`, `add_movement_input_call_node`, `add_controller_yaw_input_call_node`, `add_controller_pitch_input_call_node`)
- **FPS convenience wrappers** + closing 14/14 e2e test (BP creation → 4 InputAxis events → 5 call nodes → 4 wires → compile clean) on Mac UE 5.7.4

### Known Limitations

- **Migration tools** — no asset move / redirector fixup / dependency remap / project-version migration toolchain yet (v0.15 backlog)
- **Blueprint refactor** — no node delete / variable+function rename+delete / macro+interface editing (v0.15 chunks 5-6)
- **Get / inspect tools** — no actor get-property / get-transform / project-settings reader (v0.15 chunk 1)
- **Recipe catalog** — only 3 named recipes (`first_person_ground_character`, `widget_hud`, `mcp_self_extension_pipeline`); v0.15 adds `rts_camera`, `top_down_input`, `hud_dashboard`, `asset_naming_audit`
- **UBT target matrix** — only `mcp_build_editor`; no `build_game` / `build_server` / `build_client` / `build_packaged` (v0.15 chunks 8-9)

### How to Install

See `Docs/FIRST_LAUNCH.md` inside the source tree for the trilingual quickstart. Source users also read `Plugins/UnrealMcp/INSTALL.md` inside the zip.

The Mac source-only zip is now a **project-root overlay**: extract it next to `<YourProject>.uproject` (NOT into `Plugins/`). You'll get:
- `<YourProject>/Plugins/UnrealMcp/` — full plugin source for UBT to build
- `<YourProject>/Tools/UnrealMcpPyTools/` — project-level Python tool handlers
- `<YourProject>/Tools/UnrealMcpToolScaffoldStarters/` — canonical scaffold templates for `mcp_apply_scaffold`

Then enable both `PythonScriptPlugin` and `UnrealMcp` in `<YourProject>.uproject`'s `Plugins` array and open the project. UBT compiles the plugin against your local UE 5.6 / 5.7 install on first launch (30s–15min depending on cache).

Get-Content .\UnrealMcp-v0.14.0-python-track-full-win-ue561.zip.sha256
```
Expected: `9f80bdde2f66889415e672662ceecd27cd9eeb02f586bcbef87e9320e74c8338`

For macOS / source-only Windows clones, see the parallel [`v0.14.0-python-track-mac`](https://github.com/edwinmeng163-oss/UEvolve/releases/tag/v0.14.0-python-track-mac) release.

## UnrealMcp v0.12.1-pilot-crossplatform — Mac + Win UE 5.7 Verified

Cross-platform-verified release of the UnrealMcp self-extension workbench plugin. The plugin source content is the same v0.12.0-pilot bundle; v0.12.1 is the verification marker that adds end-to-end Windows PASS evidence alongside the existing Mac PASS.

### Assets

- `UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-mac-ue56-ue57-source.zip` — Mac-packaged source zip, ~362 KB, SHA-256 `e85e543736137ec59f5410384456dd4d1daeaa4fe39e104ae75b429a7fbc128e`.
- `UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-win-ue56-ue57-source.zip` — Windows-packaged source zip, ~360 KB, SHA-256 `aa3c624c1e5337f4a60c78ad940c05438693f00f430a16ab026247e351e2f619`. Uploaded separately by the Windows verifier.
- `.sha256` sidecar per zip in shasum format.

Both zips contain the same logical plugin source. Their hashes differ because Mac (bash + zip) and Windows (PowerShell + `Compress-Archive`) produce different archive metadata, line endings, and timestamps. Pick whichever zip matches your OS; both compile cleanly under UBT on either OS.

The plugin's internal `VersionName` is still `0.12.0-pilot` (so file names include `v0.12.0-pilot`). The `v0.12.1-pilot-crossplatform` tag marks the verification milestone, not a plugin source bump.

### Verified

- **macOS (Apple Silicon), UE 5.7.4** — clean external project from `TP_Blank`, UBT build PASS, headless editor smoke PASS, MCP `tools/list` = 111 visible tools, SIGINT graceful exit.
- **Windows 10/11, UE 5.7.4** — clean external project from `TP_Blank` (after removing `Config\TemplateDefs.ini`), UBT build PASS, headless editor smoke PASS, MCP `tools/list` = 111 visible tools, graceful `CloseMainWindow` exit.

### Verify (Mac)

```sh
shasum -a 256 -c UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-mac-ue56-ue57-source.zip.sha256
```

Expected: `e85e543736137ec59f5410384456dd4d1daeaa4fe39e104ae75b429a7fbc128e`.

### Verify (Windows)

```powershell
(Get-FileHash -Algorithm SHA256 UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-win-ue56-ue57-source.zip).Hash.ToLower()
Get-Content UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-win-ue56-ue57-source.zip.sha256
```

Expected: `aa3c624c1e5337f4a60c78ad940c05438693f00f430a16ab026247e351e2f619`.

### Install

Unzip into `<UserProject>/Plugins/` (project install, recommended) or `<UE>/Engine/Plugins/` (engine install, advanced). Open the project; UBT compiles the plugin on first launch (30s–15min depending on cache). The bundled trilingual `INSTALL.md` (English / 中文 / 日本語) inside each zip has full per-OS prerequisites and steps.

### Stage 2 reproduction recipe

For Windows verifiers reproducing on their own hardware: see [`Docs/Stage2WindowsVerify.md`](Docs/Stage2WindowsVerify.md) at this tag. The full prompt covers clone → run `Tools/package_plugin.ps1` → drop-in test → UBT build → headless smoke → cleanup.

### Not in this pilot

- UE 5.8 support comes after upstream Epic 5.8 MCP transport stabilises.
- Linux is untested.

### Known limitations (drop-in install)

- Workbench "Run Core Tests" / "Run RAG Evals" buttons are disabled unless the user copies `Tools/UnrealMcpTests/` and `Tools/UnrealMcpKnowledge/Evals/` into their project.
- `unreal.tools.import_package` returns a structured `REGISTRY_NOT_INITIALIZED` error until `<UserProject>/Tools/UnrealMcpToolRegistry/tools.json` is provisioned. The error message includes the setup recipe.

See `Plugins/UnrealMcp/README.md` and `Docs/Release-2026-05.md` in the source tree for the full pilot brief.

## 中文版

UnrealMcp 自扩展工作台 pilot 的跨平台验证版本。插件源码内容与 v0.12.0-pilot 完全相同，v0.12.1 是验证里程碑标签，新增 Windows 端到端 PASS evidence。

**资产**：
- Mac zip：`UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-mac-ue56-ue57-source.zip`，SHA-256 `e85e5437…`
- Win zip：`UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-win-ue56-ue57-source.zip`，SHA-256 `aa3c624c…`，由 Windows 验证者另行上传

两个 zip 包含相同的逻辑插件源码。SHA 不同是因为 macOS（bash + zip）与 Windows（PowerShell + `Compress-Archive`）产生的归档元数据、换行符、时间戳不同。按你的 OS 选择对应 zip；任一 zip 在两端 UBT 都能干净构建。

**验证**：

## UnrealMcp v0.12.0-pilot — Mac UE 5.6 + UE 5.7 Source Pilot

First pilot package for the UEvolve / UnrealMcp self-extension workbench. Source-only drop-in for macOS, supports Unreal Engine 5.6.1 and 5.7.4.

### Assets

- `UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-mac-ue56-ue57-source.zip` — the plugin source tree, ~362 KB
- `UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-mac-ue56-ue57-source.zip.sha256` — SHA-256 checksum sidecar

### Verify

```sh
shasum -a 256 -c UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-mac-ue56-ue57-source.zip.sha256
```

Expected: `e85e543736137ec59f5410384456dd4d1daeaa4fe39e104ae75b429a7fbc128e`

### Install

Unzip into `<UserProject>/Plugins/` (project install, recommended) or `<UE>/Engine/Plugins/` (engine install, advanced). Open the project; UBT compiles the plugin on first launch (30s–15min depending on cache). See `INSTALL.md` inside the zip — trilingual (English / 中文 / 日本語).

### Verified

- macOS (Apple Silicon), Xcode 26.x
- UE 5.7.4 — end-to-end pilot test PASS (clean external project from `TP_Blank` template, UBT build, headless editor smoke, MCP `tools/list` returned 111 visible tools)
- UE 5.6.1 — build PASS at this commit

### Not in this pilot

- Windows is not yet packaged; PowerShell equivalent of `Tools/package_plugin.sh` is the next step.
- Linux is untested.
- UE 5.8 support comes after upstream Epic 5.8 MCP transport stabilises.

### Drop-in install limitations

- Workbench "Run Core Tests" / "Run RAG Evals" buttons are disabled unless the user copies `Tools/UnrealMcpTests/` and `Tools/UnrealMcpKnowledge/Evals/` into their project.
- `unreal.tools.import_package` returns a structured `REGISTRY_NOT_INITIALIZED` error until `<UserProject>/Tools/UnrealMcpToolRegistry/tools.json` is provisioned. The error message includes the setup recipe.
- Cross-developer tool transfer happens via `unreal.tools.export_package` → gitignored `Saved/UnrealMcp/Packages/*.zip`, not by committing scaffold drafts.

See `Plugins/UnrealMcp/README.md` and `Docs/Release-2026-05.md` in the source tree for the full pilot brief.

---

## 中文版

这是 UEvolve / UnrealMcp 自扩展工作台的首个 pilot 包，仅源码 drop-in，支持 macOS 上的 Unreal Engine 5.6.1 与 5.7.4。

**校验**：`shasum -a 256 -c UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-mac-ue56-ue57-source.zip.sha256`。

**安装**：解压到 `<UserProject>/Plugins/`（项目安装，推荐）或 `<UE>/Engine/Plugins/`（引擎安装，进阶）。首次打开项目时 UBT 自动编译插件。详细安装指南见 zip 内三语 `INSTALL.md`。

**验证**：UE 5.7.4 端到端 pilot 测试通过（TP_Blank 模板新建外部项目 → UBT 构建 → headless 启动 → MCP `tools/list` 返回 111 个可见工具）。UE 5.6.1 在此 commit 构建通过。

**本次 pilot 不含**：Windows / Linux / UE 5.8。

**Drop-in 限制**：详见 `Plugins/UnrealMcp/README.md` 的 "Drop-in install limitations" 一节。

---

## 日本語版

UEvolve / UnrealMcp 自己拡張ワークベンチの初回 pilot パッケージです。ソース配布のみ、macOS の Unreal Engine 5.6.1 / 5.7.4 をサポートします。

**検証**：`shasum -a 256 -c UnrealMcp-v0.12.0-pilot-mac-ue56-ue57-source.zip.sha256`

**インストール**：`<UserProject>/Plugins/`（プロジェクト配置、推奨）または `<UE>/Engine/Plugins/`（エンジン配置、上級者向け）に展開。プロジェクト初回起動時に UBT が自動的にプラグインをビルドします。詳細は zip 内の三言語 `INSTALL.md` を参照。

**検証済み**：UE 5.7.4 のエンドツーエンド pilot テスト合格（TP_Blank テンプレートからの外部プロジェクト作成 → UBT ビルド → ヘッドレス起動 → MCP `tools/list` で 111 ツール）。UE 5.6.1 はこのコミットでビルド合格。

**この pilot に含まれないもの**：Windows / Linux / UE 5.8。

**Drop-in 制限事項**：`Plugins/UnrealMcp/README.md` の "Drop-in install limitations" 節を参照。
